Brussels Communists; Anti-Fascist Demonstration 25

(Brussels) During the opening of the International Exposition here today, over fifty Belgian communists suddenly gathered to demonstrate in front of the Italian "Riccardo" pavilion. Lallemand, a communist member of parliament, stood on the highest step of the marble staircase and gave a loud speech to the crowd, recounting the events of August 1914 (referring to the start of World War I, when German troops invaded Belgium) to compare them with the events of August 1935. He said, "Even today, the threat of war has returned, because the people of Abyssinia wish to live in peace and freedom, while Italian pan-nationalism seeks to throw them into flames and blood." At that time, leaflets were scattered, and the crowd gathered to listen at the foot of the staircase grew larger and larger. The demonstrators then broke into the main hall of the "Riccardo" pavilion. One of the demonstrators tried to destroy a portrait of Mussolini hanging in the pavilion, but Italian staff members intervened, leading to a conflict. Although it did not last long, one staff member was slightly injured in the disturbance. When the police arrived, they dispersed the demonstrators and arrested two people. MP Lallemand was also arrested but was quickly released. After this incident, the "Riccardo" pavilion was heavily guarded with increased police presence and temporarily closed for fifteen minutes. Belgian Minister of Defense; Speech on National Defense Policy 26

(Brussels) Belgium should have a well-equipped army that can quickly deploy to the front lines after a declaration of war. This is the key sentence in a radio address given by Minister of National Defense De Vrees commemorating the soldiers of the battle line. De Vrees also stated that when Belgium comes into conflict with other countries in the future, it should send its troops to the front lines rather than focus on the rear. He believes that after the national defense issue is fully resolved, a foreign invasion of Belgium will be impossible. De Vrees concluded by urging the Belgian people to recognize this need and understand the material sacrifices necessary for national defense. (5th, National Telegraph)

(Belgian Capital) Today is the anniversary of the German invasion of Belgium in 1914. Minister of National Defense Te Vandt gave a radio broadcast speech, stating, "In order to resist foreign invasions by land, we must have a well-trained army, fully equipped weapons, and a strong and agile organization. Belgium should have the border as its first line of defense, the forts built on the Haelen Plateau and the banks of the Demer River as the second line of defense, and the Meuse River, the Escaut River, and the Yser River as the third natural line of defense. We should have complete autonomy over our national defense. Only when our country is invaded by an enemy and requests assistance from friendly countries can the troops of friendly countries enter our territory. At that time, we should make preparations in advance so that the reinforcements can be sent to the front rather than retreat to the rear. If this national defense plan can proceed smoothly and be fully achieved, and if we have a well-trained and permanently serving team, then the invasion of foreign troops will be virtually impossible." (4th, Havas)

German Socialist Party Regional Congress; Goebbels' Speech; Purging Political Enemies Often Misunderstood; Asks Various Countries to Recognize Their Own Weaknesses 27

(Berlin) Labor Front leader Dr. Ley stated at the National Socialist Party Congress in Essen today that there is no need for complacency in the ranks of the National Socialist Party. Faced with a major enemy, do not be complacent or allow the dangerous situation to overwhelm you. Not everyone has the belief that the National Socialist Party will survive as long as Germany exists, and the number of those who do not hold this belief seems to be increasing daily. Hitler will not only conquer Germany but will also conquer the whole world. It is God's law that unites the people with the German leader, and this is his religion, which can move mountains. Propaganda Minister Goebbels spoke, attacking foreign newspapers, Jews, and Catholics with sarcastic remarks. He predicted that a law would soon be passed prohibiting marriage between Jews and non-Jews and that those who criticize and complain would also be suppressed. (4th, Reuters)

(Berlin) Propaganda Minister Goebbels delivered a lengthy speech at the National Socialist Party regional congress in Essen, in which he discussed the Jewish question, the church question, and the Stahlhelm question, and also made critical remarks about the attitude of various countries towards Germany. He stated, "The act of Germans marrying Jews can no longer be tolerated, as we cannot allow the mixing of German blood to be seen in our descendants. Therefore, this national struggle must continue. On the one hand, we should recognize our own strength, and on the other hand, we should recognize the enemy's tricks, so as not to be fooled by them. Foreign newspapers often misunderstand this action of Germany, thinking that there is panic within the National Socialist state, but this is not the case. What we are doing is merely a process of elimination, treatment, and purification, the purpose of which is to maintain the integrity of racial values. In the past, disputes arose because of Jewish provocations, and we have always tolerated them. Some comrades in our party can no longer understand this attitude of tolerance. In short, we should treat Jews according to how Jews treat us. For the sake of the Jewish people, since they have resided in our country, they should abide by German laws and keep themselves clean. As for the church question, we do not want to engage in a Kulturkampf (referring to the anti-Catholic movement led by Bismarck during his administration), but judging from recent facts, some people in certain aspects of the Catholic Church seem to be eager to stir up this Kulturkampf. We should wait and see how we will deal with these church figures in the coming weeks, which will not be difficult for the world to understand. In short, what we are doing is dealing with affairs in the real world, while what the church manages is the spiritual world. Therefore, it is not helpful for the church to issue newspapers and interfere in current affairs. Moreover, the National Socialist movement is the sole representative of the political will of the country. Therefore, we oppose not only left-wing political enemies but also the right-wing Stahlhelm, as we do not want them to be an obstacle to the National Socialist Party." Goebbels then mentioned the Abyssinian question and made many sarcastic remarks about the great powers, saying in essence that a few years ago, various countries signed the Kellogg-Briand Pact in Paris, opposing the resolution of international disputes through war, but not long after, the crisis of war is imminent. From now on, various governments and newspapers should shift their focus from Germany to their own domestic affairs, so that they can recognize their own weaknesses. He also said, "The act of shooting at residential houses with machine guns does not need to be sought in Germany. Germans have also never forcibly removed the flag of any foreign country (referring to the recent incident in New York where the German mail steamer Bremen had its flag removed by American communists). Only other 'civilized countries' have this 'privilege.' Moreover, the British do not need to travel across the ocean from London to Berlin to see a few broken pieces of glass in front of Jewish stores, as not far from London, in Belfast, Northern Ireland, we can openly see several houses being destroyed. As for the French, they seem to concentrate on paying attention to the substitute legal orders issued by their government regarding budget adjustments, rather than worrying about the economic panic in Germany." (4th, Havas)

(Berlin) General August von Mackensen, a famous German general during World War I who was originally a member of the Stahlhelm, recently declared his withdrawal from the group. According to the reasons he gave, since Führer Hitler took power, he has made various contributions to the country. For the sake of the welfare of the entire country, various special groups within the country are currently "not only useless but also harmful." Therefore, there is no reason for their existence. (4th, Havas)

Former German Parliamentarian Sentenced to Death for Leaning Communist 29

(Berlin) Former member of the Reichstag Keiser was found guilty of high treason by the People's Court today and sentenced to death. This is the second death sentence handed down by the court. Four other people were sentenced to imprisonment and forced labor, ranging from two to fifteen years, and were stripped of their civil rights. In the future, after being released from prison, their actions will be monitored by the police. These five people were convicted of reorganizing the Communist Party in central Germany. Keiser was detained in a concentration camp in October 1933. He was released after signing a statement that he would no longer participate in political activities. One of the defendants, a woman, was sentenced to fifteen years in prison. (5th, Reuters)

Austrian Government; Orders Prohibition of Propaganda for Restoration 31

(Vienna) The Austrian government today ordered a ban on official propaganda for the restoration of the Habsburg dynasty and prohibited local governments from granting honorary citizenship to Archduke Otto. US Senator to Recommend that the Government; Unify Governance of Territories; To Facilitate the Free Defense of the Islands; Advocates the Establishment of a Colonial Department to Centralize Authority 32

(Washington) Senator Gibson stated today that he will introduce a bill in the Senate to increase the government's control over territories and establish a dedicated colonial department. The position of the minister will be equal to that of other cabinet members. Currently, the administrative agencies for US territories are not unified. For example, Hawaii and Alaska belong to the Department of the Interior, Guam and Johnston Island belong to the Department of the Navy, and the Philippines and Panama are directly under the Department of the Army. Gibson also said that the United States is the only country in the world with such a system. The Washington Naval Treaty will expire in 1936. At that time, if the United Kingdom and Japan do not agree to renew the naval ratio system, the United States will also be free to fortify its islands to maintain its dominance in the Pacific. However, before implementing fortification, if all territories can be governed by a single department, then unified authority and progress can be facilitated. In recent years, similar proposals have been made several times, but they have not been implemented due to two difficulties: first, this plan would make the United States too imperialistic; and second, Philippine leaders oppose it because they believe this move would jeopardize the independence movement. Although the second obstacle has now been removed, the United States still retains the right to fortify the Philippines. Gibson also said that he has been studying this issue for a long time and believes that the United States should have a strong defense in the Philippines, which is even more important now than it has been in the past. (4th, National Telegraph)

Japanese Ambassador to Britain; Matsudaira's Resignation Firm; Yoshida's Succession Said to Be Powerful 35

(Tokyo) Ambassador to Britain Matsudaira's intention to resign is very firm. Former Ambassador to Italy Yoshida Shigeru's succession suddenly has momentum. The formal order will be issued approximately before November 17, when Yoshida is waiting for orders. Although Foreign Minister Hirota's efforts to persuade Ambassador Matsudaira to stay have not ceased, Matsudaira himself has decided to retire bravely at this time and must find a successor. Matsudaira himself believes that his terms of three years in the United States and seven years in the United Kingdom are too long and he is eager to give way to a worthy successor. In addition, in the disarmament conference, various parties have acknowledged his skill in requesting equal military strength last fall, and he does not delay his successful retreat, leaving room for future special tasks. Ambassador Matsudaira requested leave in July, so it will not be too late to decide whether to stay or go before February of next year. Ambassador Yoshida's waiting period expires in November, so Foreign Minister Hirota must decide on the change of Ambassador to Britain this autumn. (5th, Dentsu)

Matsuoka Yosuke Will Devote Efforts To; Economic Construction of Manchukuo; Scheduled to Cross to Manchuria on the 20th to Assume Office 36

(Tokyo) The newly appointed president of the South Manchuria Railway, Matsuoka Yosuke, is scheduled to go to Changchun on the 20th to meet with Commander of the Kwantung Army General Minami. He will seek opinions on (1) the basic principles of South Manchuria Railway management, (2) the specific principles for the economic and industrial construction of "Manchukuo", and (3) the issue of South Manchuria Railway reorganization, and express his aspirations. (5th, Nikkei)

Manchukuo Foreign Ministry; Consults on Policy Toward Russia; Border Disputes Occur Frequently; Advocates Promoting the Border Demarcation Committee 37

(Changchun) The "Manchukuo" Foreign Ministry held a plenary meeting yesterday, Sunday, in the morning and afternoon. Deputy Minister Ohashi, Chief of the Soviet-Russian Section of the European Bureau Yoshizawa, and diplomatic representatives from Harbin, Suifenhe, Daheihe, Manzhouli, etc. attended. Deputy Minister Ohashi first said that the frequent border disputes between Manchukuo and Russia are a matter of deep concern. The reason for this is the illegal border crossings and violations of the border by the Soviet-Russian side. "Manchukuo" has repeatedly issued warnings and protests. However, of the 50 incidents since the founding of the country, only 20% have been resolved. If this is allowed to continue, it will cause serious incidents in diplomatic relations and even adversely affect the peace of the Far East. Therefore, it is hoped that a fundamental policy toward Russia will be decided to ensure complete security. After deliberation, the following emergency measures were established:

(1) Regarding the protests against the Soviet-Russian side's frequent illegal border crossings, border violations, and illegal shootings, because the Russian side is not sincere in responding, the Russian side should be urged to reflect deeply. (2) In order to demarcate the border line, which is the cause of frequent disputes, it is advocated to establish a Japan-Manchukuo-Russia border demarcation committee. Japan and Manchukuo will make preparations. If Soviet-Russia hopes to resolve the matter with sincerity, a tripartite border demarcation committee will be established immediately. (5th, Dentsu)

American Magazine Satirizes the Japanese Emperor; Japanese Military Deeply Concerned 38

(Tokyo) The military is deeply concerned about the disrespectful incident involving the American magazine "Vanity Fair." This morning, Lieutenant Colonel Kimura of the General Staff Headquarters, Chief of the Special Affairs Section of the Military Police, Mr. Miza, and Major Yokoyama of the Navy Ministry all went to the Foreign Ministry to inquire about the truth of the disrespectful incident and the Foreign Ministry's policies. (Fifth day, Dentsu telegram)

(Tokyo) The disrespectful incident involving the American magazine "Vanity Fair" has prompted Foreign Minister Hirota to send a telegram instructing Ambassador Saito in the United States to call the attention of the American government. It is generally believed that the central government has the authority of publishing laws, so it is different from the problems of persecution of Japanese and Manchurian people in the western states. It should be easy to prohibit and resolve. However, the Foreign Ministry believes that the special feelings of the Japanese people towards the imperial family cannot tolerate this disrespectful incident. If the American government takes a laissez-faire attitude, it is difficult to predict whether an incident will occur due to the intensification of Japanese national sentiment. Therefore, it is planned to restrict the distribution of such magazines and demand future prohibitions. However, it remains to be seen how the American government, which respects freedom of speech, will handle the prohibition. (Fifth day, Dentsu telegram)

(New York) The American satirical magazine "Vanity Fair" recently published a cartoon about the Japanese Emperor, which has aroused dissatisfaction from the Japanese authorities. The editor of the magazine, Mr. Brownell, stated, "The American people are always able to judge cartoons appropriately. If it is published by a publication with serious content, there may be something to defend. If it is a publication that focuses on humor, like our magazine, then even if a cartoon is published, it will not cause any disputes because it has no significant meaning. For example, our magazine has published no less than ten cartoons about President Roosevelt in the past. The President has always accepted them with a smile and even purchased multiple copies of each issue to give to friends. We have never heard any criticism from him." The editor also said that only 500 copies of the issue containing the aforementioned cartoon were sent to Japan. (Fourth day, Havas telegram)

(New York) Japanese Ambassador to the United States Saito, upon receiving instructions from Tokyo, protested to the State Department about the illustration published in the famous American magazine "Vanity Fair." Japanese expatriates in the United States are angered by this illustration. This illustration clearly depicts a "historical situation that may not exist," depicting the Japanese Emperor pulling a cannon, with a certificate on the cannon titled "Nobel Peace Prize." (Fourth day, Reuters telegram)

Athens Today, 4,000 strikers on the island of Crete looted various administrative organs, injuring 30 people, including 5 policemen. Philippine Islands Trial Self-Government; Presidential Elections Next Month; Congress Adopts a Unicameral System 40

Manila The Philippines is scheduled to hold elections for the President, Vice President, and members of Congress of the autonomous government on September 17th. The Philippines has now decided to adopt a unicameral congressional system, completely abandoning the bicameral system since the Jones Act of 1916, and is closer to the parliamentary system of Spanish-speaking countries. The new Congress will have a total of 96 members, which is 22 fewer than the current number. The Philippines currently has 24 senators and 94 members of the House of Representatives. (Fourth day, Guomin telegram)

Zhejiang Provincial Government Submits Opinions on the Organization of Administrative Commissioner's Offices 50

(Nanjing) The Zhejiang Provincial Government submitted opinions on the provisional organizational regulations of the administrative inspector's office in the province. Regarding the second item, how the district security headquarters should be reformed and how to make it distinct from the administrative inspector system, the Executive Yuan ordered the Ministry of National Defense and other departments to review and reply. Three opinions have been decided: (1) The county magistrate should still concurrently serve as the commander of the security general team. (2) The district security commander is still necessary, but its organization should be specified separately from the administrative inspector's office. Whether the district security commander is concurrently held by the administrative inspector should be determined according to local conditions. (3) The Provincial Security Office should be directly under the provincial government and subject to the guidance and supervision of the central competent departments and committees. It will be presented to the Executive Yuan for review and implementation. (Fifth day, special telegram)

Shishou County Representatives Telegraphed the Whole County's Disaster Situation Shanghai Zhongbao Newspaper Office's Honorable Gentlemen, Shishou County has been hit by disasters one after another. The people of our county have suffered from the destruction of the bandits since the 19th year, and have experienced military disasters. In the 20th year, a flood caused the disaster, the dikes were breached, and the houses were in ruins. They have been displaced and suffered from repeated disasters and calamities. The people are suffering unspeakable hardships. The people have not yet recovered from their difficulties when another disaster struck. Unexpectedly, this year, a natural disaster came suddenly. At the beginning of the summer, heavy rain fell for days, and the ground suddenly dropped several feet, causing the river to rise sharply and the floods to overflow. Our dikes are mostly Yangtze River dikes, which were repaired by the Water Conservancy Engineering Department. On the 8th, the Daxingwan, Dongdawan, Huangshan Dawan, Jidiwan, and Luochengwan dikes breached one after another, affecting the entire county, inundating about 500,000 mu of farmland, and causing tens of thousands of deaths. Factories and houses were washed away, and people were displaced. According to reports from various districts and villages, the dead have been washed away by the waves, and the living are either sheltering on trees or dikes. This flood is滔天搖川漫野,畜類水中作圈,男女樹上為窠, and it is hard to find food or clothing from morning till night. All of this is the result of the collapse of the river dikes, which has caused countless tragedies in the entire county. Because the flood came so suddenly, the local area was caught off guard. The solidity of the river dikes was of no use. A safe area suddenly became a泽国. The palaces and chambers were all connected to the fishes, and the land turned into江河. It is pitiful to see the flood drowning the crops, and the people in a state of恓惶. There is nothing the people can rely on, and the villages have become like燕 without nests, and the surplus grain is ashes, all waiting to be fed. After the disaster, there is 薰蒸烈日, the 腸鳴五內, they are dwelling on ruined walls,露宿終宵, without shelter from wind and rain, and even more unable to fill their hunger. Cries can be heard all over the fields, and饿殍載道. The sight is unbearable, and those who see it lose their hearts. The pitiful survivors are垂毙, and it is difficult to go to the coming days,待振孔殷. This representative feels it is dangerous and the righteous are difficult to silence. I respectfully present the situation of the flood disaster suffered by the whole county, so that the Cí鑒 may be examined and verified. According to the express will, we safeguard the righteousness of the disaster victims and publish it in the newspaper to widely publicize it, to move the compassion of the benevolent, to invite the宏施of righteousness, to 起死回生,胜造浮亂之七级拯灾救难, and implement merits to all people. The Xinye Baihe Tanghe Lihe Tuanhe Shahe Diaohe river, folding south, runs straight through Xiangyang, and enters the Hanjiang River from Xianghe.昊天不第,久旱望雨, unexpectedly on the 4th, 5th, 6th, 7th, and 8th of this month, heavy rain poured down, non-stop day and night. 河伯肆虐, the ground rises like蛟, the flood bursts out, and the momentum is like 天降. Tens of thousands of villages were swept away, and fertile land became deserts. The rich families became beggars, and the middle-class families became饿莩. The so-called disasters in northern Hubei are all the aftermath of southern Henan, and the great flood in Hubei is also attributed to this number. We lament that the five counties suffered this鞠凶, an unprecedented catastrophe, which far exceeded Xiangzhe. However, Nanyang, Dengxian, and Tanghe were the first in the upper reaches, and the water势 was slower, but Xinye and Xiangyang

County suffered exceptionally severe flooding. The grains of wheat were gone, the houses collapsed, the people and animals drowned, and the clothing was scattered. The total loss of more than 400,000 households in the five counties is nearly one hundred and fifty million or more. The disaster is exceptionally severe and unprecedented. Two million disaster victims in the five counties are still in deep waters, without food or clothing, 風餐露宿,嗷嗷待哺,困苦萬狀,筆難盡述. People are good and benevolent, who is not as good as me,己饥己溺,谅有同情. A drop in the bucket is of little help, and a grand move depends on one. For this, we urge to allocate huge funds, or 慨解义囊, to quickly transfer them down so that they can be distributed quickly to relieve the five counties from the abyss and save the people from death. The kindness of thousands of families is immeasurable. The five counties' culture, education, and community associations thank you 敬蒸印and pay homage to the God, on behalf of the two million lives in the five counties!

Page 9

Inspection Report on Flood Disaster Areas: Special Correspondent Keng Ya for This Newspaper: Tragic Scenes in Hanchuan and Paradise in Yuekou 53

Sixty li from Xingou, one arrives at Hanchuan. Disembarking from the steamboat, one sees high and thick embankments. The entire city is submerged, yet this embankment stands alone, towering. Consequently, nearby residents have fled here to escape the disaster. Besides the existing shops, countless new straw sheds have been added, making passage for a single person difficult. At first glance, it seems like a bustling marketplace. However, upon closer inspection, nine out of ten are disaster victims struggling on the brink of death. Turning and winding through the alleys, one reaches the city wall. The accumulated water still covers two-thirds of its height. Stagnant and unmoving for a long time, the water has turned green. Tadpoles, frogs, toads, and lizards leap and swim freely. The city gate is submerged in deep water, making it impassable. However, a small boat can enter and exit through a breach in the southwest city wall. In the higher-lying streets and alleys, wooden bridges have been erected where boats cannot reach, similar to what was seen in Anqing and Jiujiang. However, the disaster situation here is particularly severe. The residents are either dead or have fled, creating a thick atmosphere of gloom.

Hanchuan's terrain is low-lying. The Xiang River cuts through the county, dividing it into northern and southern parts. Both rely on embankments for protection. On July 4th, the river water gradually rose, but the situation seemed stable. Unexpectedly, by the 8th, the Lion's Mouth in Zhongxiang, Duobao Bay in Jingshan, and Maojia Dike in this county all collapsed in succession. The water surged six or seven feet high, rushing in. The Penggong Dike on the south bank of the Xiang River, consisting of seventy-two embankments of varying sizes, plays a crucial role in preventing the Xiang River from overflowing and preventing the Yangtze River from backflowing from Dunkou. Unfortunately, the Suozi Embankment near the Xiang River also suffered a large breach, plunging the entire county into deep water. On the 13th, Nanping Dam was also breached by the Yangtze River flooding from Tunkou. The combined disaster from the Yangtze and Xiang Rivers further intensified the tragedy.

The floodwaters arrived like an avalanche, breaking into the city. It happened on the evening of the 8th. Initially, the people in the city sought refuge on tables and benches. Then, they climbed to the upper floors. Finally, they tore down doors and tiles, scrambling onto the rooftops, shouting for help. Fortunately, dawn was breaking, and the county government managed to gather thirty small boats for a swift rescue operation, transporting people to Fairy Maiden Mountain and the dike streets. Since the two locations were close, rescue was relatively easy. Therefore, although the material losses in the city were significant, no one drowned. However, in rural villages like "Tian Er He, etc.," deep within the embankments, the floodwaters surrounded and submerged the entire village. Men, women, and children were all swept away by the floodwaters, with not a single survivor. From then on, human habitation ceased. It was truly a tragedy.

According to an investigation by the Hanchuan Flood Relief Committee, the disaster area accounts for 95% of the county's area. Over 480,000 mu of farmland have been affected, with agricultural losses estimated at over 14 million yuan. Approximately 5,000 people have drowned, and there are over 360,000 disaster victims, accounting for about nine-tenths of the total population. Furthermore, the accumulated water in various places will only recede when the water levels of the Yangtze and Xiang Rivers drop by several feet. Unlike other counties where the water recedes faster and autumn crops can still be planted, the food supply here is not only a major concern now but will also be a problem next spring.

Boarding a steamboat in Hanchuan, a county official named Liu, escorting prisoners to Mianyang, said, "In this flood, the successive breaches of the embankments were partly due to the rapid rise of the floodwaters, making prevention difficult. However, it was also due to the embankment bureau's supervisors consistently neglecting their duties, failing to take preventive measures beforehand, and embezzling funds for emergency repairs. Therefore, the farmers are quite resentful and have said that if they could get their hands on Mr. So-and-So, the supervisor, they would throw him into the flood to accompany the thousands of innocent people who have drowned." In the years 1928 and 1929, Hanchuan's four rural districts were once part of the Honghu Red Zone. On the Fairy Maiden Mountain and the shores of Diaoxiao Lake, traces of past battles are still faintly visible. The farmers are straightforward and bold, which has its origins. It is understandable that they want to get their hands on Mr. So-and-So to appease their anger. However, general neglect of duty by officials should be taken as a warning.

Passing by Jinmakou, Yangchikou, Chenghuanggang, Bengkoukou, Fenshuizui, and other docks, looking out from the embankment, the disaster situation was not very evident. Nearby are six embankments: Huanggong, Hefeng, Taian, Baiyu, Xie, and Tianchi. Thanks to the county magistrate's supervision and the efforts of the villagers in emergency repairs, Huanggong Embankment was protected first, and the other five embankments safely weathered the crisis. This is the only clean land in the entire county, a testament to the idea that human determination can overcome nature. Further along to Maiwangzui, a small town also near the river, originally belonging to Mianyang, will soon be incorporated into Hanchuan. Mianyang's land is fertile, and its agricultural products are abundant. However, the continuous lakes and streams make it prone to flooding. Hence the saying: "Sand Lake and Mianyang Island, nine years out of ten bring no harvest. If there is a harvest one year, even the dogs won't eat the pot-bottom porridge." However, this year's massive floods in neighboring areas have left Mianyang unable to escape. Fortunately, the disaster area in Mianyang only reaches thirty to forty percent. One reason is that the Xiang River, after flooding from Zhongxiang, mostly flowed along the northern bank of the river. Another reason is the continuous strong south winds, which aided the water's power. As a result, the northern embankment of the Xiang River was first breached by the wind and waves, and then the floods and strong winds continued to sweep north. As a result, the disaster in northern Xiang was more severe than in southern Xiang. Most of Mianyang County is in southern Xiang, so it was fortunate to have escaped unexpectedly.

Fifty-five li southwest of Maiwangzui lies Xiantao Town, belonging to the ninth district of Mianyang County. This town has always been a strategic military location and a hub for commercial goods. It has a large population and a thriving market, and is commonly known as "Little Hankou." The steamed dishes of "Good Food Street" and the bamboo utensils of "Bamboo Utensil Street" are delicious, exquisite, and highly praised. After this major disaster, because it is a center for industry and commerce, many wealthy households from various villages have come here to reside, causing the market to become more prosperous. However, the sustainability of this prosperity may be as fleeting as the ephemerality of the night-blooming cereus. According to an investigation by the Ninth District Office of Mianyang, over 6,000 households have been flooded. The number of people affected is over 15,000 men and over 15,000 women. The losses of houses and fields are countless.

Wooden Bridge in the Streets of Hanchuan

Upstream from Xiantao, passing through places like Duoxiang River, Mayangtan, Pengshi River, Hengkou, and Shuangheyuan, most of the houses are collapsed and uninhabitable. People have temporarily built straw huts on high embankments or next to green willows as a temporary shelter to prevent future disasters. They also tie small boats to the pillars of their homes and build wooden nests high in the trees. The situation is pitiful. The breach in Shuangheyuan is about thirty to forty zhang wide and two to three zhang deep. The water is still flowing out, no wonder it has caused disaster in several counties for over ten days.

Upon arriving at Yuekou, 120 li from Xiantao, the scene is completely renewed. Shops stand side by side, and the market is bustling with people, almost surpassing Xiantao. Yuekou has an open-air theater. Previously, due to the sluggish market, there were very few ticket buyers. The livelihood of the male and female actors largely depended on the support of the stationed troops. Now, after the flood disaster, the night shows are suddenly always sold out. Various industries have also seen a turnaround. The Deyue and Cuihua Buildings, which also operate tea houses, restaurants, and bathing facilities, are tall and well-equipped. They have the air of "the wine in the jar is empty, but the seats are still full." Some wealthy merchants and large businessmen call prostitutes, sing songs, and stay up all night under the glow of kerosene lamps. In other tea houses and private homes, men and women gather to gamble on cards or play mahjong, which is common. Gambling has always been rampant in the areas along the river. However, Yuekou is a large town in a county that has been severely affected by the floods in Hubei. While the floodwaters have not receded in the four rural districts, the townspeople are so debauched, heartless, numb, and beyond reason. It is excessive.

The town has a county-run Yuekou Complete Primary School, which is relatively well-equipped, and two or three private primary schools with quite a few students. However, it seems that not much attention has been paid to social education. Because the citizens do not have access to formal newspapers, most of them gather at street bookstalls and arbitrarily purchase or listen to the reading of "Mulian Saves His Mother," "New Woman Abducts Man," "Jia's Fan Over the Tomb," "Grandpa Burning Fire," "Second Daughter Gives Dowry," and other nonsensical woodblock books. This is harmful to their minds, bodies and waste of time. I asked a bookseller, "Which books sell well?" He replied, "All books sell on normal days, but recently, 'One Hundred Lotus Flowers' have been especially popular. Each book costs 160 wen, and on average, we sell 15 or 16 copies a day." Out of curiosity, I flipped through the contents and found that it was a Qing Dynasty edition compiled for beggars to sing lotus flower ballads.

Shayang Collaborates with the People to Save the Disaster

Upstream from Yuekou, the river water gradually becomes shallower. The steamboat constantly probes the river with poles. However, it still runs aground once. The rise and fall of the Xiang River are unpredictable, and it sometimes flows south and sometimes north. The degree of curvature is often as large as a right angle. From Yuekou to Shayang, the waterway is 180 li, but according to the land mail route, it is only 60 li. Most of the waterway phenomena that hydraulic engineers consider most dangerous and undesirable can be seen in the Xiang River. The steamboat's first mate and the passengers generally believe that this is "a manifestation of the power of the river gods and demons, and there is no way to use human power to overcome nature." It is lamentable to hear this. A passenger talked about the disaster situation in Jingshan, claiming that "on July 8th at 4:00 AM, due to the breach of Dike Numbers Three and Four in Zhongxian, the floodwaters swept down Yonglong River, reaching a height of two zhang. As a result, the fourth and fifth districts of the county were most severely affected. Villages such as Xieyanggang, Guanyinge, and Yonglonghe Qiancun suffered a terrible disaster in terms of houses and population, with no one spared." He also said, "This flood was most severe in counties such as Tianmen, Hanchuan, Qianjiang, and Jingshan, all of which were once areas severely affected by the Red Disaster. Yuekou Town has a dense population, industry, and commerce. The surrounding area is known for its bandits, and security measures are usually strict. However, in 1930 and 1931, it was captured by the communists three times. In the first communist street battle, some of the remaining communists seized the bodies of those who died in battle, grabbed their legs, and dragged them away like rickshaws. In the latter two times, the number of communists doubled, forcing wealthy merchants to hand over tens of thousands of yuan in cash. They paid market prices for goods purchased in the city and for hired boat fares. The person giving orders was He Long's sister, He Ying, who was valiant, had a dark complexion, rode a white horse, and carried a box cannon, with five or six female followers. She gave speeches everywhere and was seen by many." The old wounds have not healed, and a new disaster has struck. The suffering of the people of Xiangcheng cannot be described in a single piece of paper.

Zhangjiegang is 45 li from Yuekou. The villages are about a li away from the riverbank. During the flood, people took refuge on high ground, and the straw huts they built are still new. Passing through Zekou, Huangjia, Changleyuan, and arriving at Duobaowan, the river channels are winding, and the water flows in circles. The grass, trees, and miscellaneous objects washed down from the upper reaches are hanging from the willow branches and eaves of the houses. In Duobaowan, a considerable number of human corpses were also retrieved. At one point, a male corpse was drifting near the embankment, with its arms and legs bent, floating face down like a frog. The buttocks and upper arms were particularly swollen and blood red. It seemed to be unclothed. Suddenly seeing this as the boat approached made me feel extremely uncomfortable. Remembering that on the way here, I was on the same boat as Mr. Xu Shiying's party, and we were gazing at the Yangtze River from the rail near Wuxue. Mr. Xu Gongshi once said, "The newspapers report that many corpses are floating in the river, but why haven't we seen any?" He seemed to have the attitude that one must see floating corpses to truly understand the disaster. At that time, I also thought about the saying that "male corpses float face down, and female corpses float face up." Now, seeing the tragic state of the floating corpses, I could not help but make a great vow, silently praying that I would not see them again. The first mate, perhaps aware of my feelings, smiled and said, "This is nothing. The previous times we went upstream, the men, women, children, chickens, dogs, and pigs washed down were endless. There were also straw houses or roof frames floating down, with live chickens perched on them, flapping their wings. Water buffaloes can float, and yellow cattle, dogs, and pigs that were trying to reach the embankment out of desperation have died and their bellies are swollen like drums. They drifted with the waves. When our boat first encountered the flood, it tilted and almost capsized. We quickly dropped anchor and tied it to the willows, staying there for two days and nights before we could escape safely. Although we felt sorry for the floating people and animals, there was nothing we could do to save them." After climbing the Five Sacred Mountains, one does not look at other mountains. One should not be surprised that after seeing floating corpses, many people point and sigh, while the first mate seems to see nothing at all.

Upon arriving at Shayang, the wind and waves suddenly rose, and the dry sand on the river beach was also flying and blinding. The steamboat was anchored in the middle of the river when more than ten small boats swarmed forward, all vying to help the steamboat in order to solicit passengers to the shore. Another small boat came from the shore, carrying two water police officers. One officer, tall and carrying a box cannon, and two policemen, each with short guns, were preparing to board the steamboat for inspection. Unexpectedly, when the officer was about to step onto the boat, one foot was on the small boat helping, and the other foot was still on the original small boat. The weight of the small boats was unbalanced, and the wind and waves caused it to capsize. The two police officers fell into the river, dropped their guns, and quickly clung to other boats. They were rescued by the crowd. The officer transferred his anger to the steamboat and boarded the boat to take the first mate away. Later, the "Chief of the Third Sub-Bureau" Tang Zuoxin sent personnel to investigate and clarified the truth, and announced that the first mate was innocent and released him. One of the lost guns was recovered that night. Fortunately, no water police officers drowned in this unexpected turmoil, and no innocent people were harmed.

Shayang belongs to the ninth district of Jingmen. The terrain is low-lying and suffers from floods every year. The people are experienced in flood prevention work. Although the flood overflowed into the town this time, it did not cause major damage. On July 8th, 9th and 13th, the Xiang River burst. The residents were each rowing small boats and assisting the water police to go to various villages to rescue people. Within 20 li of the surrounding area, only about ten people died. Further away, countless people drowned. The water police also worked hard to retrieve the corpses. According to statistics, Shayang retrieved more than 100 bodies, Jiukou 200 bodies, and Maliang, Sanguanmiao, etc., a total of more than 300 bodies. Most of the corpses were middle-aged men and women because they were trying to protect their property and were drowned. As for the elderly and children, they were tied high to trees in advance or sent to the roofs, so they were spared. After the 11th, the water gradually receded. Those rescued had suffered three or four days of starvation and could hardly speak. Shayang raised over 300 yuan to buy flour and steam buns to distribute. However, the amount of money was small, and the time was short. It was a drop in the bucket, and perhaps only one in ten benefited. Also, during the flood, nameplates from Nanyang County, Henan Province, were washed here, indicating the vastness of the disaster area upstream.

Shayang's agricultural products mainly consist of peanuts, sesame seeds, cotton, and grains. There are cars on land and steamboats on the water, which makes transportation convenient. There is also an electricity company. In previous years, trade was considerable. Before the disaster, the price of grain was about 8 diao per dou (equivalent to $1.10 in silver), broad beans 2.3 to 4 diao, and sesame oil 16 yuan per 100 jin. After the flood, prices have risen. Grain is now 11 to 12 diao per dou, broad beans 3.1 to 2 diao, and oil has soared to 28 yuan.

The breached dikes must be repaired quickly to prevent the so-called "New Year's rise" unique to the Xiang River at the end of winter and the beginning of spring. Also, do not use the contract system for dike repairs again, in order to save costs and reduce materials, resulting in unstable dikes and endless harm. The breach of the 72 dikes this time was precisely due to this problem. Learn from the past to avoid future mistakes. Responsible authorities, please do not disregard this advice.

Meeting of Various Agencies in Hubei Province: Methods for Dredging Rivers and Constructing Dikes; Construction to Begin Half a Month After the Xiang River Main Dam Breach; 2 Million Needed for Repairing the Zhanggong and Wuhui Dikes; Request for the National Water Conservancy Commission to Coordinate the Dredging of the Changting River 54

Hankou Correspondence: Chairman Chiang, considering the severe floods this year and the urgent need for both temporary and permanent solutions to ensure long-term relief, has issued a general order to Hunan province, instructing the construction of dikes and dams. He also called upon refugees to work on these projects in exchange for food. Simultaneously, he implemented labor conscription according to the "Regulations for People's Labor Service," promulgated by the General Headquarters. Hubei Province, located at the confluence of the Yangtze and Han Rivers, must act without delay. After receiving the order, Provincial Chairman Zhang Qun instructed the Department of Construction to convene a joint meeting with the Department of Civil Affairs, the Jianghan Engineering Bureau, and the Flood Relief General Association. Initial discussions over two days yielded no concrete solutions. At the third meeting, the following five decisions were made: (1) Dredging the Yangtze River is beyond the capacity of a single province and should be coordinated by the National Water Conservancy Commission. The Jianghan Engineering Bureau will design the dredging of the Xiang River. (2) The Department of Construction, in conjunction with the Jianghan Engineering Bureau, will conduct a survey and statistics of dikes throughout the province. (3) The Jianghan Engineering Bureau will be responsible for the repair, inspection, and maintenance of dikes and sluices. (4) Refugees in disaster-stricken areas will be employed in public works projects in exchange for food. (5) In areas with autumn harvests, labor will be conscripted according to the "Regulations for People's Labor Service" to repair dikes, following the guidelines of the Jianghan Engineering Bureau.

The Jianghan Engineering Bureau had previously received repeated orders to expedite the construction of breached dikes along the Yangtze and Xiang Rivers and had already commenced planning. It was decided to first construct the breached main dikes in the areas of Jiukou, Jingshan, and Zhongxiang on the Xiang River to prevent autumn floods. Two surveying teams were dispatched on the 2nd to conduct measurements, with construction scheduled to begin in two weeks. Other breached dikes will be repaired gradually through public works projects in exchange for food. Dikes that have not been breached will be reinforced through labor conscription. The Zhanggong Dike in Hankou, which remained intact after the flood, has been taken over by the Bureau. Today, the Wuhui Dike in Wuchang also escaped danger and was also taken over by the Bureau. Considering the two dikes as vital safeguards for Wuhan, which fortunately did not collapse, the Bureau intends to quickly reinforce the dike body and protect the dike foundation, requesting 2 million yuan for the repair of both dikes. For other dike repair expenses throughout the province, a proposal has been submitted to the National Economic Commission to allocate a ten-year fund entirely for this year's annual maintenance projects to ensure consolidation. The current flood prevention expenses amount to over 800,000 yuan. After deducting the 350,000 yuan allocated by the Economic Commission, the remaining amount will be supplemented from the surplus funds of the dike construction donation. (3rd)

Songjiang: Han Yifei Exposed for Trafficking Opium

Li Genyuan, the owner of the Yuanxing Opium Den at Xiuye Bridge outside the West Gate, was apprehended by the Public Security Bureau's special task force the day before yesterday. Five packages of private opium, bearing the Xiangtai brand, were found on his person. He claimed to have purchased them from Han Yifei. Han's hidden opium was very well concealed in a false bottom of a chamber pot in his bedroom, making it initially difficult to locate. Consequently, officers from the Second Sub-Station of the Public Security Bureau were dispatched to Han's residence, where they seized the chamber pot with the false bottom and opium paraphernalia. All items and the suspect were handed over to the county bureau and then forwarded to the county government for legal proceedings.

Caojing: Robbery and Assault

Zhu Pingsheng, a farmer from the fourth household in the third Jia of the sixth Bao in Caojing, possessed modest wealth, making him a target for bandits. Suddenly, around noon on the third, eight or nine bandits speaking a local dialect forcefully entered his home after breaking down the door. Armed with sharp knives and other weapons, they first tied up the victim and inflicted head and abdominal injuries. They then ransacked the house and fled with their loot. Upon inspection, the losses included thirty-five bolts of homespun cloth, two leather suitcases, and clothing. The incident has been reported, and an arrest warrant has been issued.

The Red Cross Society Seeks Members

The local Red Cross Society held its twelfth council meeting at the Chao Guo Temple Yilan Building (the society's headquarters) yesterday afternoon at 2 p.m. Ten people attended, including Sheng Yuanxiao, Zhu Jiuwang, and Zhou Xuewen. Sheng Yuanxiao chaired the meeting. The discussion items included: (1) A proposal to establish a membership recruitment committee. It was resolved that a membership recruitment committee would be established immediately, according to Article 1, Section 1 of the society's second membership recruitment charter. The committee would have eleven members. (2) Deciding on the committee's personnel. It was resolved that the society would appoint the county magistrate as the chairman of the committee; Zhu Jiuwang, the president of the society, as vice-chairman; Qu Bingqian as deputy chairman; Zhou Xuewen, the director of the board, as director; and Wu Cunfu, Geng Jizhi, and Zhu Guanghan as ex-officio members. Other members would be appointed by the responsible government authority in conjunction with the society. (3) Appointing a general captain for the recruitment campaign. It was resolved to nominate Sheng Jingsheng as the general captain and Yu Weigen and Huang Xiaohe as the deputy captains. Captains for each branch would be appointed by the general captain and deputy captains. (4) Determining the date for the thirteenth meeting. It was resolved to convene the meeting on the thirteenth day of this month. The meeting adjourned.

Suzhou: National Goods Store Actively Preparing for Opening

The Suzhou National Goods Store, initiated by local residents Zhang Yipeng and others, has raised 140,000 yuan and constructed a three-story steel-and-concrete building in the North Bureau area of the city. The building has now been fully completed. The rooftop of the third floor has been developed into a rooftop garden, which has already opened. The national goods store on the lower floors is scheduled to open on September 3rd. Except for some sections leased to various national goods manufacturers, the rest will be managed by the store itself. Hua Junren has been hired as the business director and is currently recruiting trainees and actively preparing for the opening.

Lawyers' Association Requests Punishment for Yixing Assessor

The Wu County Lawyers' Association, based on reports from members Tang Yingshu and others, stated that Qiu Hongzao, an assessor in Yixing County, publicly advocated for "litigation tricksters" and arbitrarily defamed the legal profession in published writings. They requested the association to forward the complaint to the Supreme Court and the Ministry of Judicial Administration for severe punishment. The association immediately raised the issue at its deliberation meeting, which resolved as follows: (1) The matter concerns damage to the reputation of all lawyers and disruption of the judicial system, making silence impossible. The association must actively advocate and forward the complaint to the court and ministry for punishment according to the law. (2) All county associations should be notified to advocate the same position. (3) Wu Zenshan and five others were publicly selected to personally petition the president of the High Court for a thorough investigation and severe punishment.

Secret Investigation of Salt Merchant Accusation

Over 150 stores, including Tongyi Refined Salt Company in Suzhou, jointly accused the Changyuan Wu Salt Warehouse in Suzhou of falsely claiming to be a charity while privately increasing salt taxes and deducting salt quantities. They filed a complaint with the Songjiang Audit Office of the Salt Administration under the Ministry of Finance. The office dispatched Lu Baomei to Suzhou for a secret investigation, which confirmed the unauthorized increase of salt taxes by 1.27 cents per unit. Consequently, Lu returned to Songjiang yesterday (5th) to report the findings.

Robbery and Assault in Suburban Suzhou

Robberies frequently occur in the four suburbs of Suzhou during the winter months. However, in the summer, when villagers often gather to chat and relax, such incidents are rare. Yet, yesterday (5th) at 1 a.m., seven bandits armed with guns, knives, and other weapons broke into the home of Cheng Xingsheng, a resident of the Cheng Anxing family in the Nan Yehong Village of Fengjia Town outside the Chang Gate. They ransacked the house and stabbed Cheng Chasheng in the leg and injured Cheng Xingsheng's mother before fleeing with their loot.

Wuxi: The Zhenxin Factory Labor Dispute Has Been Resolved

The Zhenxin Cotton Mill outside the West Gate, facing difficulties due to the high cost of cotton and low price of yarn, and exacerbated by repeated labor unrest caused by unpaid wages, had become increasingly severe. The factory temporarily suspended operations on the 1st of this month. Subsequently, County Magistrate Wang, in consultation with the Chamber of Commerce, invited Li Yunhou, the deputy manager of the Shanghai Bank; Xie Senshou, the manager of the Wuxi branch; Hua Shaochun, the representative of Zhenxin; and Cai Jianzhi, the chairman of the Cotton Textile Industry Association, to hold earnest negotiations. It was decided that the Shanghai Bank would continue to lend 15,000 yuan. Yesterday (5th), the first installment of 7,500 yuan in arrears was paid. The second installment is scheduled to be paid on the 9th. Regarding the resumption of work, the Chamber of Commerce, in conjunction with Li Tiping, Xu Chizi, and Sun Xiangfeng from the County Party Committee, agreed that the Chamber of Commerce would report the mediation process to the court regarding the Zhenxin Jiang Zeqing's lawsuit against workers Wu A'da and others for damage and injury. Additionally, Zhenxin will file a motion to withdraw the lawsuit after slightly reorganizing the factory internally, and resumption of work will be scheduled for ten days later.

Public Security Sub-Bureau Chief Accused of Neglect of Duty

Over 100 merchants and business firms outside the South Gate, including Tang Baoru and Pu Shuying, accused Tong Zhongyue, the chief of the Third Sub-Bureau of Public Security, of greed and neglect of duty, leading to lax policing and a series of robberies and murders, leaving the local public with no security. They convened a meeting the day before yesterday and unanimously decided to petition the County Government Public Security Bureau to promptly dismiss and severely punish him. Failing that, they would elect representatives to petition the provincial government. They have already collected evidence and submitted it to the County Government Public Security Bureau, requesting a thorough investigation and punishment to uphold the law.

Changzhou: Three Districts Report Drought and Famine

Wu Zongjin, the director of the Third District of Wujin County, reported that since the beginning of summer, the six townships and towns of Longting, Renxing, Shiqiao, Mengcheng, Zhengli, and Wansui in the district have experienced scarce rainfall, totaling less than 0.5 Chinese feet. The water in the ditches and ponds has long been evaporated by the intense sun. Currently, bean seedlings are withering, and rice seedlings are scorched. All types of red, green, and black beans, sesame, and other crops are damaged by leaf rollers, black cutworms, and other pests. A plague has broken out, and the future harvest is hopeless. Yesterday (4th), he specially reported to the county government, requesting the swift dispatch of personnel for on-site inspection and relief efforts.

Notorious Bandit Liu Huancan Arrested

Liu Huancan, a notorious bandit from Liujiatou on the border of Wujin and Wuxi counties, has committed numerous crimes. He was involved in the robbery of the Fei family in Jiangtou Village of the Sixth District. Despite orders for his arrest, he remained at large. Recently, the criminal secretly returned to his village and was detected by Inspector Zhu Sen of the Donghenglin Police Station. Zhu led police officers to arrest him and transported him to the County Public Security Bureau on the 4th, before transferring him to the County Government for interrogation.

Jiangyin: Appeal to Revise the Publication Law

The Wuxi Xin News Reporters Association, in order to appeal to the central government to revise the publication law, held a meeting last month and decided to solicit the unanimous support of colleagues from various counties south of the Yangtze River. The local press expressed strong support and decided that Xi Xiaohua from the Zhengqi Newspaper and Cao Yichen from the Dasheng Newspaper would go to Wuxi on the 9th to participate. On the 10th, they will join representatives from various counties in Wuxi to petition in Beijing.

Nantong: A Promising Cotton Harvest

In the counties under the jurisdiction of Nantong in Jiangbei and the coastal reclamation areas of Huainan, although the cotton planting initially suffered from drought, subsequent heavy rains and hot summer weather with a suitable balance of sun and rain have led to excellent cotton seedling growth. The cotton plants are now blossoming and forming bolls, promising a full harvest. The market is showing positive signs due to the expected bumper harvest of new cotton in the autumn.

The Nantong District Commissioner's Position Remains Vacant

Zheng Yitong, the administrative inspector of the Nantong District, has left Nantong to take up a new position as a member of the provincial government. His duties are currently being handled by Secretary Zheng Yu. Peng Zhaoxian, the newly appointed commissioner, has been reassigned as the Director of the Civil Affairs Department of Shaanxi Province. The replacement for the position remains undetermined.

Haimen: Notorious Opium Trafficker Arrested

Zhang Yuncheng (from Ziyang, Shandong Province, currently residing in Hexi, Haimen County), a notorious opium trafficker in the county, has been trafficking and selling private opium in various districts for years, amassing significant profits. Due to his careful planning, he has never been caught. On the morning of the 3rd, Zhang transported a large quantity of private opium from Shanghai by sea and landed at Niuhong Port. About a mile north of the port, he was stopped and inspected by police officers Zhang Yucheng and others from the Public Security Bureau, who found his bags suspicious. The bags were full of private opium. Zhang and the contraband were immediately taken to the bureau and transferred to the County Anti-Opium Committee in the afternoon for interrogation.

Yangzhou: Five-Colored Stone Lotus Blooms at Faha Temple

In the bamboo forest of Faha Temple on the banks of the Slender West Lake in the northern suburbs of Yangzhou, an unusual flower has suddenly bloomed, with five colors on one stem, said to be auspicious. Visitors come morning and evening to admire it. The red flower gradually turns into tender pink, tender yellow, tender green, ocher yellow, and powdery white, all five colors. The stem is straight, and the petals are shattered, with five segments. The petals resemble velvet embroidery and seem to speak in the wind, captivating observers. Some people identify it as Qionghua, but it is uncertain whether that is the case.

Lawsuit Against Widow for Arranging Granddaughter's Marriage Without Consent

Wu Youchao, a farmer from Caowang Township in the county, filed a lawsuit because his widowed daughter-in-law, Wu Xiao, had been living separately since her husband's death. She inherited thirteen and four-tenths acres of land and an orphaned daughter, Yu Mei. Currently, Ms. Wu is involved in an affair with Chen Songxiu. The land has dwindled to only eight acres, and she intends to marry Yu Mei (age seven) to Chen Songxiu's son. Citing Article 973 of the Civil Code, which prohibits marriage contracts for girls under the age of fifteen, Wu Youchao went to court yesterday (3rd) to request that Ms. Wu be summoned to court to legally prohibit the marriage and to determine guardianship of Yu Mei. A mediation hearing is scheduled for the 10th.

Pinghu: Pedestrian Killed by Car on Highway

Since the opening of the Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway in Zhapu, incidents of pedestrians being injured or killed have occurred frequently. Two accidents occurred last month, both resulting in fatal injuries. On the afternoon of the 31st, Zhang Shouchun, residing on Hosiery Factory Street in the South City of Shanghai, was driving his private car with Shanghai license plate number 7362 when he struck and killed Bao Shunhe, a 66-year-old pedestrian, near Longwangtang in the Zhapu jurisdiction. The Second Public Security Sub-Bureau, upon learning of the incident, impounded the vehicle and telegraphed the county government for instructions. Yesterday, County Magistrate Zhang Zhouwen personally went to collect the body.

Jiaxing: Agricultural Bank Prepares for Agricultural Warehouses

The Jiaxing County Local Farmers Bank, in order to regulate rural finance and increase the price of agricultural products to maintain farmers' livelihoods, plans to establish seven agricultural warehouses this year, one each in Xinsheng, Xinfeng, Wangdian, Wangjiangjing, Yuxian, and Youchegang. Preparations are currently underway to enable farmers to store various grains and miscellaneous grains in the warehouses and sell them when prices are favorable. Furthermore, Manager Shen Xian'en believes that the bank's operations have been significantly hampered by the past embezzlement and escape of former manager Wu Heshu, despite reorganization by the Construction Department and gradual recovery. Past loans amounted to 30,000 to 40,000 yuan, and efforts are being made to recover them to improve financial flexibility. The bank is also seeking loans from other banks to establish mortgage loans as soon as possible. With the early rice harvest approaching and rice prices declining daily, the agricultural warehouses in Wangdian and Yuxian will be established first to allow farmers to obtain mortgages.

Hangzhou: Reconnaissance of the Fujian-Jiangxi Railway Completed

The Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway Council, following a telegram from Chairman Chiang instructing the Council to examine the proposal from Chen Yi, the Chairman of the Fujian Provincial Government, to extend the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway from Jiangxi province to Fuzhou in Fujian province, dispatched a reconnaissance team led by Wang Xiuqin in early June. The team traveled from Shangrao through Fujian, passing through Yanping and arriving in Fuzhou. The reconnaissance has now been completed, and the team returned to the province yesterday. According to reports, the entire line is over 300 kilometers long, traversing high mountains and steep ridges, making the project extremely difficult. The estimated construction cost is approximately 22.2 million yuan. A measurement cost budget will be prepared to conduct surveying, with funding to be provided by the Fujian Provincial Government, to facilitate construction.

The Autumn Incense Market in the City is Quiet

The autumn incense season in Hangzhou is upon us. The Provincial Highway Bureau has opened a special bus route from Hubin to Dongyue Temple to facilitate travel. However, due to the economic downturn and the collapse of the rural economy, the number of pilgrims is extremely small, resulting in reduced temple revenues and a quiet market. Business for shops is slow, and the Highway Bureau has reduced the frequency of special bus trips. Daily ticket revenue is only around one hundred yuan, less than half of last year's figure.

Xiaoshan: Locusts and Rice Borers Found in Cotton and Rice Fields

Cotton plants cultivated in the Xiaoshan East Township Improved Cotton Area have been found infested with "seed hopper nymphs" that feed exclusively on cotton leaves. In areas such as Changshantou and Yujiatan, most of the cotton leaves have been eaten. Early rice in sandy areas has also suffered significant damage from rice borers. While people are catching the pests, they cannot be eradicated entirely. Additionally, rice borers have been found feeding on rice in the inland rice patties, but a heavy rain on the 3rd, which lasted all day, raised the water level in the fields to half a foot, killing most of the rice-eating insects. Farmers were overjoyed.

Tragic News: Wife Murdered After Gambling Losses

In the Xinlin Village area of Xiaoshan East Township, a merchant named Zheng Jimin was addicted to gambling. In recent days, he repeatedly lost, totaling over 500 yuan. On the morning of the 3rd, he demanded jewelry and silverware from his wife, Ms. Wei. When she refused, he repeatedly stabbed her with a kitchen knife, inflicting five fatal wounds. Neighbors reported the incident to the local police, who then reported it to the county government for an autopsy. Zheng, realizing the enormity of his crime, fled alone towards the Nansha area.
