China-British Boxer Indemnity Board of Trustees: Approves Huai River and Guangdong-Hankou Railway Loans; Allocates 600,000 Yuan Each in September and October; Approves Additional 750,000 Yuan for Huai River Project; Approves Ministry of Education's Request for Additional 50,000 Yuan in Aid for Moral Education 55

According to the Shenshi News Agency, the China-British Boxer Indemnity Board of Trustees convened expanded finance committee and education committee meetings in Shanghai starting on July 26th. The 32nd plenary meeting of the Board of Trustees was held yesterday morning, discussing and approving major proposals submitted by the finance and education committees, including loans for the Guangdong-Hankou Railway and the Huai River Commission. Details are as follows:

Finance Committee Resolves Various Proposals

The expanded finance meeting of the China-British Boxer Indemnity Board of Trustees was held at 5:00 PM on July 26th at No. 6 The Bund, Shanghai, to discuss the loan issue for the Guangdong-Hankou Railway. Attendees included Yan Deqing, Chen Qicai, Marshall, Zeng Rongpu, and others, with Zeng Rongpu chairing the meeting. The meeting discussed the Ministry of Railways' proposal to borrow 2.2 million yuan in Boxer Indemnity funds to address the urgent need for construction funds for the Zhuzhou-Shaoguan section of the Guangdong-Hankou Railway. It was resolved that, after reviewing categories 3 and 5 of the loan agreement for the completion of the Guangdong-Hankou Railway, no further loans were available except for those already allocated and designated for the Public Debt Fund, and the 500,000 yuan approved at the 69th meeting of the expanded finance committee to be allocated in early August. The expanded finance committee suggested allocating 600,000 yuan monthly starting on September 10th from Category 4 loan funds.

Education Committee Resolves Cases

The 21st meeting of the Education Committee was held on August 3rd. Attendees included Li Shuhua, Zhu Jiahua, Liu Ruiheng, Dai Leren, Song Ziliang, and others, with Li Shuhua chairing the meeting. Key proposals were discussed and resolved, including: (1) A request from National Sun Yat-sen University for a portion of the 40,000 yuan annual subsidy to be allocated to the University's Soil Survey Institute. It was resolved to allocate 10,000 yuan annually from the university's subsidy for the current and following years to the College of Agriculture's Soil Survey Institute. (2) A proposal from the National Central Research Institute's Physics Institute to expedite the construction of factory buildings, utilizing equipment funds from the 24th year of China-British Boxer Indemnity subsidies. It was resolved to approve the proposal. (3) A request from Guangxi University for a subsidy for the equipment of the Mineral Processing Laboratory of the Mining and Metallurgy Department, based on the estimated cost table submitted. It was resolved to approve the subsidy. (4) Rules regarding graduation and thesis fees for government-sponsored students studying in the UK. It was resolved that master's graduation and thesis fees would be 15 pounds, and doctoral graduation and thesis fees would be 20 pounds. (5) A telegram from Education Minister Wang requesting additional funds for moral education. It was resolved that this committee considers the proposal of national educational policies to be of utmost importance, and having already been discussed and resolved at the joint meeting of the Boxer Indemnity agencies last year, the outcome of the discussion suggests that this situation is different from ordinary requests for funding. The Board of Trustees is advised to allocate half of the funds to Qinghai and half to Ningxia. However, this is a special situation and shall not be used as a precedent for any subsequent requests.

Plenary Meeting Held Yesterday, Board of Trustees Meeting. The 32nd plenary meeting of the Board of Trustees was held yesterday, attended by Zhu Jiahua, Marshall, Yan Deqing, Zeng Rongri, Liu Shuhua, Chen Qicai, Liu Ruiheng, Song Ziliang, Jing En, Candler, Wilkinson, and others, totaling eleven members. Hang Liwu, the Director-General of the Board, and Shen Shihua, the Director of the General Affairs Department of the Ministry of Transportation, were present as observers. Zhu Jiahua chaired the meeting, and Zheng Baozhi recorded the minutes.

Passes Motions for Loans to the Huai River and the Guangdong-Hankou Railroad

The meeting began at 9:00 AM yesterday and concluded at 1:35 PM, passing critical motions, including (1) the motion to approve an additional loan of 750,000 yuan for the Three Gates project of the Huai River Commission. (2) The Guangdong-Hankou Railway Zhuzhou-Shaoguan section funding motion, resolved to allocate 600,000 yuan in both September and October. (3) The motion to allocate grants to Guangxi University, Zhejiang University, and Xiangya Medical College, resolved to allocate as requested. (4) Motion for the date and location of the next meeting, resolved to hold the regular meeting on September 14th and the Board of Trustees meeting on the 16th, both in Nanjing.

Farewell to Government Funded Students Studying in the UK

24 students were granted government funding to study in the UK from the China-British Boxer Indemnity fund and are scheduled to depart for the UK today aboard the British Mail Ship "Kayson." The Board hosted a farewell party yesterday afternoon at the residence of Mr. Wilkinson, 1925 Xiafei Road. Attendees included Board members Zhu Jiahua, Song Ziliang, Zeng Rongpu, Chen Aishi, Liu Ruiheng, Mayor Wu Tiecheng, the British Consul General in Shanghai, and Marshall, the President of the British Chamber of Commerce. Zhu Jiahua and Wu Tiecheng delivered speeches, and a student representative responded. The party ended around 7:00 PM. The list of students receiving Boxer Indemnity funding this year includes Qian Zhongshu, Zhang Wencai, Qian Baojun, Zhang Chenghong, Su Guangfu, Wang Zushun, Shi Zhengxin, Zhang Yi, Wu Zhongxian, Xu Shaobin, Zhu Baoxian, Xie Mingshan, Peng Shulin, Zhu Tingfeng, Mao Derong, Zhang Zhao, Yang Zengwei, Cheng Yuqi, Li Huazong, Ke Zhao, Jin Ruihuang, Zhang Wenyu, Yang Renjie, and Zhang Wenzhi, totaling 24 individuals.

Mayor Wu Delivered Farewell Address Yesterday

According to the Central News Agency, the China-British Boxer Indemnity Committee selected 24 students to study in the UK this year. They were given a farewell tea party by Mr. Marcel, the Vice-Chairman of the Committee and President of the British Chamber of Commerce. Following a speech by Zhu Jiahua, Chairman of the Board, Mayor Wu delivered the following address: "I am very honored to have the opportunity to attend the farewell party for this year's students going to study in the UK and to say a few words at this grand gathering. You must know that the difficulties China is currently facing are like what is described in ancient Chinese poems, 'A leaking house suffers from continuous rain, and a broken boat faces headwind.' These two lines of poetry not only symbolize China's current difficulties but also deserve to be a constant reminder for every patriotic Chinese. To resolve these difficulties, we must begin with the wisdom of the people, a unified will and action, patience, and prolonged effort. Your most important goal and mission in studying in the UK is to prepare to resolve these difficulties and build a new China. When our Chinese youth go abroad to study, their purpose is to learn from others' strengths and make up for our own weaknesses. Therefore, what we should study and research is not the prosperity of foreign countries today, but how foreign countries have become strong. China and the UK have a long history of friendly relations, and the UK has many things we can learn from. I hope that when you return to the country after completing your studies, you will not only make valuable contributions to the country and society but also enhance the intimacy of Sino-British relations. There are not many Chinese youth with the opportunity to be educated, and even fewer who can go abroad to study. We who have the opportunity to be educated, and especially those who have the opportunity to receive foreign education, should serve our compatriots who do not have the opportunity to be educated. Therefore, I often say to Chinese students, 'Now is the time to build houses, not to live in them; now is the time to cook food, not to eat it.' So, I cannot help but take this opportunity to express my hope that you will serve the country and society in the future, build houses for the people, and cook food for the people. Farewell, everyone, goodbye, everyone. I hope you will remember my sincere and earnest farewell words today, and work hard and cherish our difficult and struggling motherland."

Silk and Tea Exports Gradually Thrive; Tung Oil Shipments to America are Most Numerous 56

The price of Chinese silk abroad has been steadily declining, leading foreign merchants to halt their operations. Although the government has encouraged exports and attempted to improve silkworm varieties, it has been unable to restore the industry to its former state. However, in recent months, European and American countries have begun to purchase Chinese silk again. Last month, French company postal ships transported a total of 1,500 to 1,600 bales of Chinese silk to Europe. British company postal ships also shipped over 900 bales, and Blue Funnel Line and Japanese postal companies also each shipped several hundred bales.

The largest shipment by a French postal ship, containing over 800 pieces, marks the largest amount of Chinese silk exported in recent years and suggests a revival in the foreign demand for Chinese silk. Shipments to America are also simultaneously improving. Last month, Jardine Matheson & Co. shipped over 500 pieces of Chinese silk to New York. The amount transported by the Ch'ang Hsing Company to Vancouver and then to America was roughly equal. As for Chinese tea, exports to Europe have slightly increased, with shipments primarily going to Kashmir. Recently, a Blue Funnel Line ship exported 1,200 tons of tea valued at 700,000 to 800,000 yuan. Today, the British postal ship Kaiserieh departed for Europe with over 100 tons of tea. In America, tea exports remain sluggish, but there has been a large increase in tung oil shipments recently, with over 100,000 barrels already exported.

Hsu Shih-ying's English Talk: Flood Relief Matters - Continues to Visit Financial and Charitable Circles, Deciding to Hold a Joint Meeting to Plan Emergency Relief 57

Hsu Shih-ying, Chairman of the National Government's Relief Commission, returned from inspecting the disaster areas in the Yangtze River provinces. For two days in Shanghai, he separately instructed Mayor Wu and financiers and philanthropists such as Chang Kung-ch'uan to discuss raising funds for flood relief. He has been extremely busy running around and appealing for millions of disaster victims. A reporter from the Hsin Sheng News Agency visited Mr. Hsu at Renji Hall yesterday and was received for a detailed discussion of the negotiations of recent days. Details of the situation are recorded as follows:

Support from All Sectors

Mr. Hsu stated, "Since returning from inspecting the disaster areas in the Yangtze River, the lives of millions of disaster victims have been constantly on my mind. Yesterday and the day before, I visited Mayor Wu twice but did not meet him, as the Mayor was out on official business. According to his family, he will return in the evening, and I will contact him by telephone. In addition, I visited Chang Kung-ch'uan, Ch'ien Hsin-chih, Lin K'ang-hou, and others from the financial sector in Shanghai, as well as philanthropists Wang I-t'ing, Wen Lan-t'ing, Huang Chin-rong, Tu Yueh-sheng, and others. All have expressed unanimous support and generously donated. Therefore, there should be no difficulty in raising funds for relief in the future."

Holding a Meeting

"Now that this matter has the support of all sectors, it has been decided to hold a joint meeting of all sectors to discuss the progress of fundraising. The joint meeting is scheduled to be held this Thursday (August 8) at 4:00 PM at Renji Hall. The name will be the Shanghai Flood Relief Association for Various Provinces. Its organization and fundraising methods will be streamlined and implemented aggressively following the previous methods used by the Drought Relief Association, because although the number of disaster victims is very large, many are in danger of not making it to the next day. Therefore, this relief effort is urgent."

Inviting Mei to Perform

Mr. Hsu also stated, "The night before last, I accepted an invitation from Li Shih-tseng to attend a banquet at the World Academy for Mr. Mei Lanfang, who had returned with acclaim. At the banquet, I described in detail the severity of this year's flood and the suffering of the disaster victims. All the guests present unanimously supported the idea of inviting Mr. Mei to stay in Shanghai to advocate for millions of disaster victims and raise funds through performances. The performance period is set for one month. The start date and performance location have not yet been determined, but will likely wait until the New World's flood relief entertainment is over before setting a date to begin. Whether it will be at New World will be discussed and decided at that time."

Leaving Shanghai on the Tenth

"As for inspecting the Yellow River flood areas, I have decided to depart from Shanghai on the tenth, taking a ship to Qingdao and then transferring to the disaster area. The duration is set for two weeks. If time is not sufficient, it will be extended temporarily. The joint meeting of the Relief Association will be held on the eighth and will likely be established. Therefore, leaving Shanghai on the tenth will mark a small break in my efforts for the relief effort. After inspecting the flood in the Yellow River area, I will return to Shanghai to continue working hard on the relief effort."

City Center - Railroad Fully Completed - Opening to Traffic Before the Opening of the National Games on October 10 59

A reporter from Shen Shi News Agency met with Xiao Wei-kuo, Director of the Two-Road Traffic Department, yesterday. According to him, the city government, in order to facilitate transportation in the city center, has jointly built a railroad in the city center with the Ministry of Railways, starting from the Kaochingmiao Station on Sung-Hu Road, along Sanmin Road to the intersection of Wusong Road, with a total length of over two kilometers. The construction cost is over 40,000 yuan and is being built by the Two-Road Bureau. Construction began in the spring of this year, involving 4,200 cubic meters of earthwork, the construction of two wooden bridges, and one station building and platform each. It is now fully completed and awaiting the Ministry of Railways' approval before officially opening to traffic. It is expected to be open for passenger traffic before the opening of the Sixth National Games on October 10.

Industrial and Commercial Credit Loans - Loan Committee Reviews and Approves - Rejections for Non-Compliance - Mortgage Loans Negotiated with Banks and Firms 60

Since announcing the review of small credit loans on August 1, the Shanghai Industrial and Commercial Loan Review Committee has been handling matters in accordance with the ten principles promulgated by the Ministry. As for mortgage loans, factories negotiate with banks and firms themselves. Details are recorded as follows:

Credit Loan - Review and Approval

Industrialists and businessmen have been enthusiastically obtaining application forms for small credit loans from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce. It is reported that the Loan Committee initially sent 3,000 application forms to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, which have already been used up. The committee approved the Municipal Chamber of Commerce's two requests for additional forms yesterday and sent another 1,500 copies for distribution. However, there are not many who have submitted completed forms to the committee. It is reported that several of the applicants are not engaged in the production of national goods. According to the loan regulations, "loans are limited to factories manufacturing national goods, shops selling national goods, and those transporting national goods for export," so they fundamentally do not qualify for loans. In addition, several factories have applied for loans that are several times their own assets, which is inconsistent with the ninth principle of the ten loan principles promulgated by the Ministry, "the total amount of loans shall not exceed half of the factory's capital and public reserve." It is reported that the committee will reject such applications in accordance with the regulations and hopes that applicants will pay special attention to the regulations and the explanatory notes issued by the committee to facilitate the process. Furthermore, according to the person in charge of the Loan Committee, the committee will handle applications fairly in accordance with the regulations and procedures and submit them to the committee meeting for decision. Factories should formally apply to the committee in accordance with the procedures and do not need to seek help from individuals to save time.

Mortgage Loan - Negotiated Independently

After the Industrial and Commercial Revival Committee of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce approved inquiries from various industries regarding mortgage loans of 15 million yuan, it sent a letter to the Loan Review Committee urging inquiries. According to a reporter from the Hsin Sheng News Agency, according to Article 2 of the loan details, "the total amount of industrial and commercial mortgage loans is limited to 15 million yuan, which will be lent by banks and money shops themselves, but must be reported to the committee for review and national treasury certificates will be issued as the second guarantee for the loan in accordance with the loan amount." Therefore, these loans should be negotiated directly between factories and shops and banks and money shops. It is reported that several factories and shops have directly negotiated with banks and money shops. After negotiation, they will report to the committee for review and issuance of national treasury certificates.

North German Lloyd's Second Express Ship - Potsdam's Arrival in Shanghai - Invitation to Visit on the Seventeenth - Shanghai-Europe Tickets Sold Out 61

The German Second New Transport Potsdam is the second of the three ships in the North German Lloyd's Central Europe Express service. The shipowner is Hapag-Lloyd, which was merged into North German Lloyd by order of the German government to facilitate unified management in business. Potsdam is also a specially built new ship, and its equipment and layout are all designed to suit the Far East route. Like the North German Lloyd's Scharnhorst, the ship has first class and economy class passenger seats. Since the route must pass through the tropics, special attention is paid to ventilation and heat resistance. Since its first voyage from Germany on July 5, the schedule has been delayed by ten days due to receptions and visits being held everywhere along the way. The Shanghai Melchers & Co. received a telegram from the shipowner Olendorff yesterday stating that the ship will arrive in Shanghai on the seventeenth and will still dock at the Kung Ho Hsiang Wharf. The ship plans to invite visitors from all walks of life and will depart for Japan on the nineteenth. The ship is slightly smaller than the Scharnhorst, with a net tonnage of 17,518 tons, a length of 193 meters, a width of 22.5 meters, and the same speed as the Scharnhorst. Passenger seats to the Far East are full, and first class and economy class cabins from Shanghai to Europe have all been pre-purchased.

Municipal Land Bureau - Reorganizing Shanghai Land - Clearing 75% of the City's Area - Developing Land Certificate Areas Covering One Hundred and Five Maps 65

The Municipal Land Bureau has been actively carrying out the reorganization of land in Shanghai for several years. The information obtained from the bureau is recorded as follows:

Clearing 75% of the Area

It has been over seventy years since land was cleared in Shanghai in the fifth year of Xianfeng (1855), and the boundaries of people's fields have not been accurate, and the boundaries of maps have been lost and difficult to verify. Moreover, the area of ​​Shanghai includes the former Baoshan and Shanghai counties, so the names of the maps are inconsistent. To facilitate organization and benefit the people, all the original bao tu wei numbers in the cleared areas will be abolished, and new divisions will be made based on natural boundaries, and map names will be compiled. Land certificates will be filled in accordingly in the future. Currently, the Zhenru, Wusong, Gaoqiao, Jiangwan, Yinhang, Pengpei, and six districts in the former Baoshan area have been cleared by the Baoshan Land Clearing Bureau. A part of Wusong Jiangwan belongs to the war zone and has been re-measured. A part of Yinhang District belongs to the city center area and has also been re-measured. Other areas such as Zhenru, Pengpu, and Gaoqiao have also been re-measured due to road construction and requisition. The seven districts of Hunan, Caojing, Fahua, Yinxiang, Yangsi, Zhabei, and Tangqiao have all been measured. Yangjing and Pusong are currently being measured. The total cleared area accounts for approximately 75% of the city.

Property Evidence Collected Uniformly

Shanghai is an industrial and commercial port, and the evidence of land ownership is extremely complicated. Therefore, the bureau has collected all the original property evidence and issued land occupation certificates. However, due to the different natures of the various documents, the certificate replacement procedures are also slightly different. In the cleared area, each household's map will be drawn first, the area calculated, and the plot number assigned. The bureau will then announce the certificate replacement and order the people to bring various documents and grain certificates for the past three years to the bureau within the specified time to identify the single map. After signing and recognizing, the certificate will be issued. Each certificate will be attached with a map, and the terrain and four addresses, as well as the location of the land and the location of the entire area, will be clear at a glance. The number of acres is accurate, and the evidence is unique, so the land certificate is the only proof of property rights in the city. There are now one hundred and five areas that have been measured and developed for land certificates, and approximately 110,000 certificates have been issued.

The Riverbank Base Will No Longer Be Used

Land prices in Shanghai are expensive, so if ownerless land is discovered during the clearing, or if people report the encroachment of public land, it will be taken over by the city after verification. The land taken over can be requested for sale, or it can be leased to the people to avoid waste and benefit the income. As for the old riverbank base, it is stipulated that all those with a length of more than 500 meters and a width of more than one meter are public riverbanks, and those that do not meet the above regulations but are indicated in the deeds held by the owners are private riverbanks. This public riverbank was indeed needed in the past, but the current situation has changed, and fields have become thoroughfares. The old riverbank base will no longer be used and can be taxed by the owners on both sides. If the owners on both sides give up their rights, it can be taxed by a third party. There are also extra land surcharges and beach surcharges.

Overseas Chinese Expelled from Japan - Petitioned the Municipal Government Yesterday - Overseas Chinese Affairs Bureau Sent Representatives to Comfort - Three More Expelled Overseas Chinese Arrived 66

After 71 overseas Chinese who were expelled from Japan returned to China on the China Revival Company's Hua Wu ship, they were temporarily staying at the Jiangxi Guild Hall. Zhabei Textile Factory - All Factories to Resume Work Today 67

The 18 silk factories in Zhabei suddenly experienced a strike on the morning of the third, causing all 18 silk factories to be shut down. Party and government agencies paid close attention to this matter and sent personnel to investigate in detail. The Silk Industry Association convened a meeting at the association hall the day before yesterday and decided to listen to the handling of the matter by the party and government authorities. Yesterday, the 10 silk factories north of the railway were restored to work, while the railway factories remained shut down. Yesterday morning, the chairman of the association, Shen Huachen, went to the Municipal Party Headquarters and the Bureau of Social Affairs to ask for guidance. Party and government agencies believed that the matter should be resolved quickly and ordered the factories to open today and notified the workers of all factories to resume work, while notifying the local military and police agencies to protect them, so it is expected that all factories will resume work today.

Representatives of Hubei Native Place Association Discuss Relief Methods with Hsu Shih-ying 68

The Hubei Native Place Association established a Flood Relief Association the day before yesterday. Chairman Han Juemin reported on the preparations for the Flood Relief Association. It was generally believed that the disaster area in Hubei this time was as wide as 51 counties, with hundreds of thousands of disaster victims and a large number of people drowned. The loss of cotton, grain, and miscellaneous grains was approximately 200 million yuan. The disaster was serious and unprecedented. Chairman Hsu Jingren of the Accounting Committee was asked to investigate despite the summer heat and did not hesitate to work hard. As a senior citizen of venerable age, he traveled thousands of miles, traced up the Jingjiang River and down the Xiangjiang River, and personally oversaw the situation. This attention to the disaster area was unprecedented and was a savior for the people of Hubei and a lucky star for Jianghan. It was resolved that Tang Zhuxin, Yin Guanzhi, Han Juemin, Liu Wanqing (replaced by Peng Yuncen), and Lu Xingjie would be publicly elected as representatives to thank Chairman Hsu and ask about the impressions of the disaster area and the current and future relief methods. Chairman Hsu replied, "The Jingjiang and Xiangjiang rivers are connected by the sky and water, and it is difficult to distinguish north from south. Except for the treetops, the parapets, and the roofs, it is a vast expanse of water. The tragedy is heartbreaking and indescribable. Three methods have been proposed for post-disaster relief: emergency relief, agricultural relief, and industrial relief. The funding for emergency relief belongs to the local government and is for setting up porridge kitchens, building shacks, selling cheap grain to relieve hunger, and providing medicine to prevent epidemics. The funding for agricultural relief belongs to the provincial government and is for distributing seeds, replenishing agricultural implements, and opening farmers' banks for lending. The funding for industrial relief belongs to the national government and is for dredging waterways and building trunk dams and people's dams. Emergency relief and agricultural relief are the standard for water management, and industrial relief is the basis for negotiating water. They will be carried out in order to save the natural disaster in the future." The representatives believed that what Chairman Hsu said was a good plan for saving lives and was a permanent solution, with good laws and intentions, and the same contribution as Yu and Ji. They hoped that he would preside over the implementation and save the common people, and thanked the 30 million people of Hubei. The chairman replied, "I will do my best and exhaust my strength." The representatives were satisfied and left.

Sino-Foreign Relief Association - Continued Reports of Disaster Situations in Various Places 69

The Sino-Foreign Relief Association on Renji Road received many letters and telegrams from various places requesting relief for flood disasters yesterday. They are summarized as follows, hoping that philanthropists at home and abroad will act with compassion and generosity to help the survivors of the disaster avoid sinking into misery: (1) Yuan'an, Hubei: The county currently has more than 20,000 people waiting for assistance, unable to live or die. The sound of fathers and mothers crying for their children and the groans of starvation can be heard everywhere, and suicides by hanging and drowning are common sights. (2) Jingsha: (omitted) Jingsha was struck by a natural disaster, with floods overflowing, and hundreds of thousands of lives were in ruins, half buried in the bellies of fish and half as mourning wild geese. At present, the disaster victims should be gathered, waiting to be fed. Although Shabu is a rice-producing area, it is now a time of scarcity, with rice reserves exhausted and sources cut off. If this continues, they will all perish. (3) Shishou: Historically remote and barren, located in the lower reaches of the Jingjiang River, statistics show that 80% of the county was flooded, with more than 5,000 people drowned, more than 400,000 mu of farmland submerged, and more than 30 million yuan of property lost. Since 1927, Shishou has suffered from successive soldiers and bandits, as well as the great flood of 1931 and the severe drought of 1934. This year, it has suffered this tragedy again. There is not only no empty house, but also no field of green grass. Children cry and women wail, with no way to find food. (4) Sheng Lu, Anhui: Since the summer, the river tide has risen sharply and mountain floods have broken out. The Yonggu, Tianbao, Dacheng, Sucun, Yongfeng, and Lotus weirs, as well as the various dikes along the river, have been tragically destroyed one after another. Livestock have been swept away, and houses have been destroyed. Tens of thousands of people have suffered the same catastrophe, eating grass and sleeping in the open, and the sound of lamentation is unbearable to hear. The county suffered from drought last year, and the livelihoods of farmers were already unsustainable. Now, the houses and crops have been swallowed by the flood. Food and shelter are not available, and they are repeatedly devastated. The state of hunger and separation is extremely miserable. What is the crime of the people, to suffer this disaster? (5) Shimen, Hunan: The current flood has stretched for about 400 miles and is about 100 miles wide. About 5,600 houses have been destroyed, nearly 200,000 mu of farmland have been destroyed, and about 10,000 people have been drowned. The severity of the disaster is even greater than that of Tianmen and Xiangyang counties in Hubei. About 60,000 to 70,000 people are in urgent need of relief.

County Affairs:契稅 Land Deed Tax Reduction Extended for Another Two Months 73

The Shanghai County Government has received instructions from the Finance Department of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, roughly stating: the tax rate for land and property deeds has been reduced to 6.3%, and the original surcharges must not exceed half of the regular tax. The deadline for this extension was the end of July this year. However, as it is currently the lean season and the social economy is in difficulty, many white deeds have not been taxed in time. If the extension and reduction are not considered, it will inevitably lead to a wait-and-see attitude, which is not conducive to increasing tax revenue and benefiting the people. Now, starting from August, the extension will be extended for another three months, until the end of October. The original surcharges are still not allowed to exceed half of the 6.3% tax rate. After receiving the order, County Magistrate Ye issued a notice to the public yesterday to inform them. The continuation of the extension and reduction this time is intended to show consideration for the people's livelihood. It is imperative to take advantage of this extension period to pay taxes on all untaxed deeds, and there should be no further delays.

After Yu Qiaqing Resigned, the Work of the Shipping Cooperative Was Suspended; Authorities Still Hope for Continued Active Progress 74

The specific plan for China's shipping cooperation, formulated by the China Shipping Cooperation Design Committee after six months of research, has been promulgated by the Ministry of Communications and the board of directors of the China Shipping Cooperative has been established. Subsequently, due to obstacles, Executive Director Yu Qiaqing resigned in anger, resulting in a suspension of work. The details are as follows:

Work Suspended After Yu's Resignation: After the establishment of the board of directors of the cooperative, it planned to establish (1) a Joint Business Office for Yangtze River Steamers, under which all regular liners operating on the upper, middle, and lower reaches of the Yangtze River and the Shanghai-Ningbo line would be affiliated; (2) a Joint Business Office for Coastal Steamers, under which all regular liners and non-regular liners operating to ports in the North and South Seas and non-regular liners operating on the Yangtze River would be affiliated; (3) a Business Office for Port Steamers, under which all regular liners operating to ports not designated as treaty ports would be affiliated. For several months now, due to practical obstacles, it has been impossible to implement. Executive Director Yu Qiaqing resigned in anger, resulting in a suspension of the cooperative's work.

Various Companies Adopt a Wait-and-See Attitude; Cooperation Difficult: The reason for the suspension of shipping cooperation is that state-owned and private shipping companies cannot effectively cooperate. For example, each company, due to local historical route relationships and slightly different business practices, is unwilling to share all of its special interests with the public. At the same time, they are deeply afraid that the cooperative will be controlled by a small number of people. After its implementation, the original personnel of each company will inevitably be eliminated. Therefore, various companies have adopted a wait-and-see attitude, and some parties have intentionally delayed, making it impossible to implement in practice. However, in order to plan for shipping cooperation, the authorities hope for continued active progress in order to achieve the goal.

It is also heard that the reorganizers and others will begin work immediately, re-registering those members who were previously omitted from registration, and plan to actively complete the reorganization work in the shortest possible time, which will definitely bring new achievements to the labor movement on the two railways.

A Woman with a Mental Illness Committed Suicide 80

A man surnamed Ye from Hunan, residing at No. 20, Fuchang Lane, Linqin Road, West Gate, currently works as a secretary in a certain agency. His wife, Ms. Wang, 22 years old, recently suffered some kind of mental stimulation for unknown reasons. The day before yesterday, she secretly ingested morphine. When the poison took effect and she began moaning, she was taken to Renji Hospital for treatment by car. However, due to the passage of too much time, it was impossible to save her, and she soon died. Yesterday, her family coffined her and transported her to the Chaozhou-Nanxun Guild Hall on Xieqiao Road in the South City for temporary placement. When passing near the West Gate, a police officer noticed and asked for a certificate for transporting the coffin, but there was none. He ordered them to first transport it to the guild hall and reported the information to the West Gate Branch Bureau, which ordered the local bailiff Lu Zhaoxiong to report to the local court and request an autopsy. Later, Prosecutor Xie Lian led Examiner Shen Qixiu to the scene for an examination, which confirmed that she had died from ingesting poison. The cause was filled in, and the coffin was resealed, pending further instructions.

Opening of the National Goods World; He Bingxian Opens on Behalf of Chen Gongbo, Hu Die Cuts the Ribbon; Water Disaster Propaganda Meeting of the Citizens' Association Also Opens Simultaneously 83

Only then can the country and the people become strong." Opening Declaration

The opening declaration of the world stated, "Military aggression is certainly enough to destroy a country, but economic aggression is also enough to destroy a country and exterminate a race. Our country, under the economic aggression of the great powers, is also encountering floods and droughts, which have led to rural bankruptcy, industrial and commercial collapse, and a general state of depression in all aspects of society. To save the country from such a national crisis, in addition to using customs policies to curb foreign economic aggression, we must also cultivate the psychology of the people of the country to love and use national goods, so that national goods can be sold vigorously in the market. After blocking the loopholes, we can talk about all other national salvation policies. Shanghai is the largest port in China, with a population of 3.5 million, holding the hub of national culture and economy. Its every move is enough to make the whole country follow suit. Our world is based on this principle, uniting more than 100 famous national goods factories to sell exquisite daily-use national goods, serving as a medium between production and consumption, in order to achieve equal supply between production and consumption, so that industry and commerce can be revived and finance can become stable. We hope that wise men and pioneers of national goods at home and abroad will work together to achieve this. We hereby declare."

It is truly a scene of misery everywhere. Because Shanghai has not suffered this catastrophe, the general public is still indulging in extravagance and singing and dancing all night long. It is truly what is called 'A merchant girl does not know the hatred of national subjugation, and still sings the backyard flower across the river.' It is truly sighing. The Citizens' Association has initiated propaganda for this purpose, hoping that all sectors will donate generously."

Central Shanghai 87

The Complex Case of a Woman's Corpse Retrieved from the Huangpu River: Three Laborers Describe Witnessing the Victim's Murder; Another Girl Also Thrown into the Huangpu River Simultaneously 88

On the third of this month, at 2 PM, as the Beiyang-class Shengjing ship berthed at Pier No. 3 of the Taikoo Dock in the French Concession was raising anchor to leave the port, its propeller's rotation suddenly churned up an unidentified female corpse. The lower body was naked, and medical examination revealed signs of redness, suggesting a possible murder. However, valuable jewelry and over one hundred yuan in banknotes from various banks that she carried were not taken. After the corpse was retrieved by the Customs Water Police, detectives were dispatched to investigate this suspicious case, details of which were reported in this newspaper previously. After the occurrence of this case, the day before yesterday evening, an elderly woman from Suzhou, Zhang Zhou Shi, along with her daughter-in-law, Zhang Li Shi, went to the South City Rescue Bureau claiming that after reading the newspaper today, the description of the deceased strongly resembled their niece. The bureau then had the corpse brought out, and Zhang Zhou Shi positively identified her without mistake. That evening, they reported to the Customs Water Police requesting the arrest and prosecution of the murderer. They provided a detailed account of the deceased's life, stating that the deceased was named Zhang Jinlin, 48 years old, from Suzhou. When she was 29, her first husband passed away from illness. Later, she became involved with a Shandong man named Mou Jia, leading to disdain from her in-laws and uncles. She then followed Jia to Shandong and opened a silk shop in Kaifeng Prefecture, which gradually prospered and became quite profitable. The deceased once brought two thousand yuan to Shanghai, deposited it in a comb shop in this port, obtained a deposit book, and collected interest annually. She now has a ten-year-old daughter in Shandong. Recently, the deceased came to Shanghai alone, withdrew two hundred and sixty yuan in interest from the shop, and then engaged in an affair in Shanghai, forgetting to return to Shandong. She and her lover bought utensils and planned to rent a house to live together. Recently, she suddenly did not return for two nights, and unexpectedly, she died in the Huangpu River. After receiving the report, the police department intensified its investigation. Yesterday morning, they brought in three dockworkers from the Taikoo Dock, Hao Zhongyang, Zhuang Changshou, and Qi Jinbao, who claimed to have witnessed the victim's murder. They all stated that at around 11 PM on the second of this month, they were cooling off on Taikoo Pier No. 3 when two men and a woman suddenly appeared with a six- or seven-year-old girl to stroll around the pier. After wandering around on the Shengjing ship for a week, they returned to the pier. Then, they saw one of the men angrily scold the woman and use a wooden stick in his hand to hold her down and strike her head violently. The woman pleaded in vain, and then another man instructed the woman to take out dozens of yuan to settle the matter, but the assailant refused, insisting that unless the woman was killed, his own safety would not be guaranteed. After arguing until midnight, they forced the woman to take off her Xiangyun silk pants and, taking the opportunity, violently pushed her into the Huangpu River. The six- or seven-year-old girl wanted to cry for help but was also thrown into the river by the man. Both of them did not resurface. The three of them intended to use bamboo poles to rescue them, but the assailant pointed a pistol at them, making it impossible to save them, and they watched the two men flee. After obtaining these statements, the police department deemed the case complex. The reason for the woman's murder and the identity of the girl who was killed at the same time were still difficult to find clues for. In addition to sending the three witnesses to the local court for questioning first, at 11 AM, they sent personnel to report to the court, requesting an official to examine the corpse, ordering the family members of the deceased to prepare a coffin for burial, and waiting for the arrest and prosecution of the murderer.

Tricked by Someone: Two Foremen Slashed; No Automobile Accident; Disaster Struck En Route to Negotiations 89

Li Jining from Hangzhou, 36 years old, residing at No. 3, Mingyue Lane, Qiwupu Road, has been working as a deputy foreman at the Zhonghua No. 1 Knitting Factory on Longjiang Road, Yangshupu. Yesterday afternoon around 4 PM, while Li was still working in the factory, he suddenly received a phone call from outside the factory, claiming that his brother, Li Jishou, had been hit by a Southern automobile near Dongxin Bridge and that the injured person had been sent to the Southern Automobile Head Office at the intersection of Xihua De Road and Huade Road, waiting for Li Jining to negotiate compensation for medical expenses. Upon receiving this news, Li Jining, deeply concerned for his brother, became extremely anxious and went with the factory's head foreman, Wu Donglin. However, both Li and Wu were unfamiliar with the route, so upon arriving near Zhuangyuan Mansion, they became lost and immediately asked a man in short clothes at the entrance of the lane for directions. The man also claimed not to know and told them to inquire with another man in short clothes at the entrance of the lane ahead. Li and Wu, without suspecting anything, followed the instructions. Upon reaching the location, the man in short clothes immediately pulled out an iron rod from behind him and violently struck Li and Wu. Li Jining and Wu Donglin, caught off guard, were struck one after the other and fell to the ground, screaming for help. Nearby patrol officers, hearing the alarm, rushed to the scene, but the assailant had already fled. They then transported the two to Tongren Hospital for treatment. Li Jining's leg was the most severely injured, with his foot bone having been broken. Wu Donglin was also injured in the leg. As for the incident of Li's brother, Li Jishou, being hit by a car, after police investigation, it turned out to be completely fabricated. The victims also did not recognize the assailant's face. According to bystanders, it was speculated that someone who had a grudge against Li had devised a plan to retaliate by falsely reporting an accident, luring him out, and carrying out this vicious act. The police are currently pursuing the matter.

French Concession: Cracking Down on Re-rolled Cigarette Butts; Considered a Hindrance to Public Health; Those Arrested Fined One Yuan Each 90

Western officers from the Sanitation Department of the French Municipal Council, in view of the fact that in recent years, the stalls selling re-rolled cigarettes along various roadsides were all set up by impoverished and idle people who specialize in collecting leftover cigarette butts picked up from the roads or garbage dumps, taking them apart and re-rolling them to sell to others, which seriously hinders public health and abnormally crowded the roadsides, especially notified the French police to crack down and arrest them. The remaining defendants were each fined one yuan, and if they were to perform labor service, one yuan would be deducted for one day. The rolled cigarettes and other items seized in the case were confiscated and burned.

Lost Eight Yuan, Committed Suicide at Home with a Knife; Borrowed Money from Relatives to Treat Illness; A Tragedy Occurred After the Money Was Stolen 91

Chen Huabao, a 26-year-old farmer from Caohujiazhai Village, Paotai Bay, Wusong, made a living by farming. His parents passed away early, and he married Shen Shi, who was of similar age. They had two sons and one daughter, all of whom were young children. Huabao had been suffering from tuberculosis for many years, which led to poverty in the family. Recently, his old illness recurred. The day before yesterday, he borrowed ten yuan from relatives to treat his illness. This morning, he went to Songzhen to buy vegetables, spending two yuan. The remaining eight yuan was placed in his pocket, intending to see a doctor in the afternoon to treat his illness. However, he was pickpocketed at the vegetable market, and the thief stole the money. When Chen realized that the money was stolen and tried to investigate, the thief had already disappeared. He returned home with tears in his eyes and cried loudly. The neighbors all knew that he had been robbed, but they did not expect that there would be an accident. Unexpectedly, after crying, Chen thought to himself, "I am already plagued by illness, and I hate the ruthlessness of the thief." In anger and resentment, he conceived a world-weary thought and took advantage of the fact that his wife and others were working in the fields, and committed suicide with a sharp knife in the house, stabbing himself seven times all over his body. He immediately fell dead on the bed. At noon, his wife, Shen Shi, returned home for lunch and, not seeing her husband's face, went to the room and saw her husband lying face up in a pool of blood. She called out to him, but he did not respond. In panic, she rushed out and called the neighbors, and went back to look closely and saw that Huabao's whole body was covered in blood and his breath had been cut off for a long time. At this point, Shen Shi realized that her husband had committed this tragic murder due to the stolen silver. Although she was heartbroken, she had no one to raise her children. She could only prepare a coffin for burial.

Huang Shengda Dies Tragically after Being Slashed by an Enemy; Suspect Song Guanlong Arrested; Bloody Axe Found 92

Huang Shengda, 36 years old, from Changzhou, had been running a round wood shop at No. 98, Fuling Road, and also contracted to make wooden barrels in the Chinese Nail Factory at No. 85 on the same road, so business was not bad. It was recorded that at around 3 AM the day before yesterday, Huang and his wife, Zhang Shi, were sleeping on the floor in front of the shop when someone broke in and slashed Huang's right temple with an axe before escaping. Huang's screams for help woke Zhang Shi and others, who saw that her husband's head was already bleeding profusely, but the murderer was nowhere to be found. They immediately went out to report to the Chinese police and called for an ambulance by telephone, which rushed him to the Sacred Heart Hospital for treatment. After being informed, the Yulin Road police station dispatched detective Jin Wanrong to the hospital to investigate. Huang stated that he did not see the murderer's face when he was slashed, so he did not know who it was, but he had never had any feud with anyone. Only Song Guanlong (currently residing at No. 8, Beijie, Yinxiang Port) in the same industry had previously contracted the wooden barrels of the nail factory together, but recently Song had been dismissed by the factory, so all the wooden barrels were made exclusively by Huang. Therefore, this assassination was likely committed by him. After hearing the statement, the detective immediately went to the address and arrested Song, and found an axe with blood stains at the scene. He was brought to the police station together and prepared to be sent to the court for detention and investigation today (the 6th). The axe was also sent to the Municipal Council's chemical testing office to test the blood stains. Huang died in the hospital due to the severity of his injuries, and the treatment was ineffective. He passed away at 3:15 PM the day before yesterday. The body was transported to the Felun Road autopsy station. Yesterday morning, Guo Wei, the prosecutor from the Special No. 1 Court, along with forensic doctor Zhang Yan and secretary Wang Zuyi, came to the station to examine the body. According to the report from Western police chief Beikesi, Song Guanlong, 43 years old, from Chuansha, who runs a round wood business, denied having any feud with the deceased and also denied slashing him with an axe. The rest of the statement was inconsistent. Huang Zhangshi, the wife of the deceased, stated that although she was sleeping with her husband at the time, she did not see who the murderer was and requested an investigation. After receiving the statement, Guo Jun issued a statement that the deceased, Huang Shengda, male, was indeed killed by a sharp instrument during his lifetime, and the suspect Song Guanlong was handed over to the police station for investigation before being sent to the court for verification. The body was handed over to his wife, Huang Zhangshi, for burial after signing a guarantee.

Ministry of Communications Holds National Radio Registration; Promulgates Provisional Registration Measures; Registration Began Yesterday 96

The Ministry of Communications, in view of the fact that radio receivers have been installed freely and without restriction in shops, factories, and homes in various provinces, cities, and counties across the country, in order to facilitate management, has specially promulgated provisional registration measures and is holding registration, which began yesterday. Details are recorded as follows:

Application for Registration

The application form for registration of radio receivers issued by the Ministry of Communications states: "It is hereby declared that so-and-so, residing at such-and-such address, has installed a so-and-so type of radio receiver. All machine program and other items are listed below, and we are willing to abide by the provisional registration measures for installing radio receivers that have been promulgated. We respectfully request registration and the issuance of a registration certificate. To the Ministry of Communications, applicant so-and-so, signature and seal." The registration form includes: (1) type of machinery, (2) number of vacuum tubes, (3) antenna style, (4) current supply situation, (5) wavelength range, (6) use of headphones or amplifier, (7) purchase or self-assembly, (8) machine value, (9) factory name, (10) store name of sale.

Registration Information

(1) All households should obtain the registration application form from any of the following radio stations under the jurisdiction of the Ministry of Communications and fill in each item in detail: Shanghai, Nanjing, Hangzhou, Ningbo, Dinghai, Chongming, Wuhu, Hankou, Wuchang, Shashi, Yichang, Changsha, Qingdao, Jinan, Yantai, Weihaiwei, Luoyang, Zhengzhou, Tianjin, Beiping, Xiamen, Fuzhou, Nanchang, Guangzhou, Shantou, Chongqing, Chengdu, Wanxian, Xuzhou, Guiyang. (2) The method of filling out the registration application form is listed as follows: (A) Under the item of machine type, the entry should indicate whether it is a crystal set or a vacuum tube set. If the name of the circuit adopted can also be indicated at the same time, it will be even better. (B) If the machine is a vacuum tube set, the number of vacuum tubes should be noted. (C) Under the item of antenna style, the antenna installation form, number of roots, length, etc. should be noted. (D) Under the item of current supply situation, the current used in groups A, B, and C, or whether it is city electricity or batteries, should be noted separately. (E) Under the item of wavelength range, the wavelength range of the radio receiver used, which can receive radio waves from so many meters to so many meters, should be noted. (F) Under the item of machine value, if the machine is self-assembled, the total number of purchases of each component should also be noted.

Yangtze River Imports: Lightships Temporarily Replaced with Gas Buoys 97

Shipping Notice No. 1070 from the Maritime Division of the Inspectorate General of Customs: It is hereby announced that the Yangtze River Import Lightship, which is anchored at the import location in the south waterway of the Yangtze River and belongs to the Jianghai Customs, must be temporarily removed for repairs due to collision damage, and replaced with a gas buoy to facilitate navigation. The substitute buoy is decorated with horizontal red and black stripes and equipped with a white intermittent flashing light, flashing once every eight seconds, with each flash and pause lasting four seconds. The relevant map is Chinese Navy Hydrographic Chart No. 1011. In the future, when the lightship's repairs are completed, it shall be returned to its original location to resume normal service, and the substitute buoy shall be removed (no separate announcement will be made at that time). All shipping merchants are hereby notified to be aware of this announcement. August 1, 1935, Carnell, Port Officer, Maritime Division

Marrying a Wife with Unknown Origins; Turns Out the Matchmaker Designed the Enticement and Sale 101

Hou Bosheng, a villager from Caigenglang Wangjiaku, Hongqiao, West Shanghai, married Xu Caibao, the younger sister of Zhu Zhang Xiuying, a woman from Pinghu, as his wife through a matchmaker on the sixth day of the first lunar month this year. He paid 180 yuan as a tea gift, and they immediately married. Unexpectedly, after half a year, Xu Mingsheng, a man from Pinghu, reported to the Beixin Jing Police Station that his cousin Xu Caibao had been designed and enticed to be sold by Zhu Zhang Xiuying, requesting detention and investigation. Following instructions, the police dispatched officers to detain Zhu Zhang Xiuying, Hou Bosheng, Xu Caibao, and others and send them to the local court. After investigation by Prosecutor Zhang Zi, he ruled that Xu Caibao be taken back by Xu Mingsheng, Zhu Zhang Xiuying be detained, and Hou Bosheng be released on bail, and filed a lawsuit with the criminal court. Yesterday, Judge Wu Deying specially opened the 12th court to hear the case. First, the plaintiff Xu Mingsheng testified about the previous situation, requesting legal action. When questioned, Zhu Zhang Xiuying, 26 years old, admitted that she was a matchmaker, but denied enticing Caibao, and the rest of her statement was evasive. Hou Bosheng testified that he was 25 years old and that Chen Quantang's wife came to him as a matchmaker on the third day of the first lunar month, talking about Zhu Zhang Xiuying, who opened a teahouse a short distance from my house, having a younger sister who was intended to be married to me, and agreed on a tea gift of 180 yuan. On the sixth day, my family used a sedan chair to carry Xu Caibao home, and I really didn't know that Xu Caibao had been enticed by Zhu Zhang Xiuying. The official asked them since they were sisters, why did they have different surnames? Hou replied that Zhu Zhang Xiuying said she was her maternal uncle's daughter. Finally, Wang Jianchun, the lawyer hired by Hou Bosheng, rose and defended for a long time. The judge said that the case was clear, so he concluded the hearing and awaited sentencing. Zhu Zhang Xiuying was sent back to custody to await instructions.

Oriental Hotel Guest Suicide: Reportedly Due to Economic Hardship 103

Yesterday morning around two o'clock, a tea server on the fourth floor of the Oriental Hotel on Xizang Road suddenly noticed a guest in room 463, named Wang Jifu, 30 years old, from Ningbo, tossing and moaning in his room. He knocked on the door, but there was no response. Sensing something was wrong, he quickly opened the door and entered, only to find the guest pale and unconscious. He immediately reported this to the police station, who dispatched a car to take him to the hospital for treatment. Unfortunately, due to severe poisoning, he could not be saved and soon died. The body was sent to the coroner's office for a special examination, while the family of the deceased was being investigated. The cause of the suicide was reportedly due to economic hardship. Before his death, he had worked as a clerk at the Ruifeng Exchange Shop at the intersection of Fujian Road and Hankou Road.

Apprentice Electrocuted to Death 104

Yin Husheng, a local resident, 19 years old, was an apprentice at the Xiesheng Safe Deposit Box Shop on Oujia Road. Yesterday afternoon, around eight o'clock, after Yin finished his dinner, he and other fellow apprentices went outside to cool off because of the hot weather. Because it was dark, the group suggested finding a way to connect a light outside. Yin was instructed to fetch an electric wire to connect to the power. Carelessly, Yin touched the live light socket with two fingers. Instantly, the electric current threw him several feet away, electrocuting him to death on the spot. Other fellow apprentices saw this and rushed to check on him, but he was already dead. They immediately reported it to the police station, who transported the body to the coroner's office for examination.

Jin Hui Association: First Inaugural Ceremony for Elected Staff 105

For the purpose of mutual encouragement, the fellow villagers from Jinjiang and Hui'an counties of Fujian Province established the Jin Hui Association, which has lasted nearly a hundred years. In order to promote the association's affairs, the fellow villagers from these two counties decided to switch to a membership system. After being guided by Party and government agencies in accordance with the law, the first session of staff members was elected. At two o'clock in the afternoon on the fourth of this month, the inaugural ceremony of swearing-in was held in the auditorium of the Eight Immortals Bridge YMCA. More than twenty people attended, including Wang Longzhang, a representative from the Shanghai Municipal Party Headquarters, and the association's staff members Tang Jingsong, Chen Cheng, and Wu Zemin. The executive director of the association, Chen Cheng, read the oath, and the Shanghai Municipal Party Headquarters representative, Wang Longzhang, separately oversaw the swearing-in. The ceremony was grand and orderly. Afterwards, Wang Longzhang, representative of the Municipal Party Headquarters, exhorted them to work diligently and serve the interests of their fellow villagers. Subsequently, the executive director of the association, Chen Cheng, delivered a thank-you speech, and then they took photos and had tea before dispersing.

Electrical Industry Association Publishes New Book 106

The National Federation of Private Electrical Industries has recently published a technical monograph entitled "Calculation Method for High-Voltage Line Electrical Engineering." The book was written by Mr. Qiu Shien, director of education at the Electrical Industry Correspondence School. The content details the calculation method for the electrical permanent phenomenon of high-voltage AC transmission lines. The material is rich and the solutions are innovative. It is a basic book for studying high-voltage AC transmission and is most suitable for use as a reference book for universities and vocational schools in China. It is reported that the book has already been published and is priced at five jiao in silver dollars per copy. It can be purchased directly from the Electrical Industry Correspondence School at 212 Nanjing Road in this city. Students of the school can get a 20% discount.

Li Shaoguang Offers Reduced-Fee Medical Treatment 107

Li Shaoguang, a mental health therapist currently residing at 41 Huayuanfang, Jinshenfu Road, had already engaged in the study of mental medicine during his studies at Southeast University. After more than ten years, his experience and knowledge have become extremely rich. He has a unique understanding of various modern mental therapies. Since Zhao Hengti, Xu Shiying, Zhang Taiyan, Du Yuesheng, Wang Yansong, and other famous figures in the country persuaded him to stay in Shanghai to practice medicine, three years have passed, and his achievements have been outstanding. All those who have received his treatment have seen remarkable improvements. Moreover, he does not haggle over consultation fees. In the past, when Sun Houzai's wife suffered from tuberculosis, hemoptysis, and severe chest pain, Mr. Li braved the wind and rain to treat her, and she recovered after ten treatments. Not only did he not receive any payment, but when they were in dire straits, he lent them a dozen silver dollars to help them through their difficulties. Sun, originally from Zhejiang, had fallen into the officialdom. The elderly couple had never met Li before, but they were introduced by a friend. He is so chivalrous and his intention to save the world is commendable. It is now heard that Mr. Li, recognizing that illness is a significant loss to mankind, and that nine out of ten cases can be cured without medication, and in light of the current economic downturn, many poor patients suffer and ruin their futures due to the high cost of medicine, he has decided to offer reduced-fee medical treatment starting from today. Except for Sundays, there will be morning clinic hours from 9 AM to 12 PM, with only a registration fee of four jiao in silver dollars, and medical fees are waived to benefit the poor. In the afternoon, from 1 PM to 4 PM, there will be regular clinic hours with a medical fee of one yuan. The fee for house calls and long-distance treatment is also one yuan, which is also an affordable price. However, for special appointments, the consultation fee is still five yuan, and the house call fee is ten yuan. All of the above registration fees are as usual.

The Great World Implements a Policy of Accessibility to the Common People 108

The Rongji Great World is Shanghai's only mass entertainment venue. With low ticket prices and a variety of performances, it attracts visitors like rivers flowing into the sea. Therefore, its business is very prosperous. In the past, this amusement park employed male and female tea servers, distributed throughout the venues, to serve guests and offer tea, for the convenience of visitors. Unexpectedly, these tea servers have recently dared to secretly demand exorbitant tips. When the management of Changfa discovered this, they immediately dismissed all of them and closed the tea rooms to avoid extra expenses for visitors. If visitors want to quench their thirst, there are economical fragrant teas available for only one copper coin per cup. This is truly a well-deserved policy of accessibility to the common people. Therefore, the Great World has become even more lively recently, and many people go to the rooftop to cool off in the evening.

Characteristics of Domestic Cotton Yarn 109

The cotton yarn used for sewing comes in two sizes: 200 yards and 500 yards. Although someone in our country had previously started a business for the 200-yard size, it ultimately failed due to its inability to compete with foreign goods. Several companies in our country have started businesses for the 500-yard size, and the best of them is the Red Lion brand. The 500-yard foreign cotton yarn was originally capable of being defeated by domestic cotton yarn. Unexpectedly, recently there have been imported goods being dumped on the market at very low prices. The sales methods are also meticulous. The future of our domestic cotton yarn is truly worrying. Recently, it has been heard that the manufacturers of the Red Lion brand cotton yarn, in view of this situation, have carefully studied and reduced production costs so that they can offer the same price as imported goods. The cotton yarn products were launched on August 1st.

Chunqiu (Spring and Autumn - magazine supplement of the newspaper)

Anecdotes 117

— (Pianyue)

An honest woman, in her youth, seeks a reliable husband to entrust her life to, believing that this will ensure her long-term future stability. A cunning woman, though sharing the hope for long-term stability, would never decide on her nominal husband in her youth. She would rather invest more in cultivating and elevating her own reputation and status, enjoy all the material and spiritual offerings that men bestow upon a young lady, and all the grand honors that society bestows upon a famous woman. Only then, before being abandoned by the times, would she choose her final destination: marrying a husband sought after by the masses but difficult to obtain.

People of the present often lament "the decline of social morality" or praise "the revival of ancient ways," mostly holding a psychology of valuing the past over the present, using the past as a mirror. But if one examines the customs of ancient times and the behavior of the ancients, they also mostly valued profit over sentiment, and those who did not follow the ancient ways were the majority. If one traces back to the most ancient times, it was a world where knowledge was undeveloped and only brute force and aggression were valued. It is evident that every generation is merely influenced by the prejudice that "distant monks are better at chanting scriptures," using the facade of valuing "ancient ways" to measure the present.

Random Thoughts on the Double Seventh Festival 118

— Qiulang

Among the many seasonal festivals, yesterday's Double Seventh Festival (Qixi), is the most poetic and sentimental. Perhaps it is because the myth of the Cowherd and the Weaver Girl is constructed with extreme skill, and the plot is so sad and beautiful. It is no wonder that the general public of emotional young men and women express sympathy and pray to the stars for skill. We do not need to study the meaning and value of this myth now, but we have two feelings about it:

Let us temporarily follow the legend of the myth: the Celestial Granddaughter and the Cowherd, because they owed the Heavenly Emperor a hundred thousand wedding money and were unable to repay it, the Heavenly Emperor exercised the authority of a creditor! He punished them by making them farm and weave all year round, separating them on opposite banks all year round, only allowing them to meet once on the Double Seventh Festival. We can know that being in debt is the most painful thing in the world, and creditors will oppress and bully them in heaven and on earth! If a person can be diligent and thrifty in life and not be in debt, then he can obtain true freedom.

As for praying to the stars for skill, it is also a mistake! Although it is a game, it requires reality. Think about it, they are separated all year round, and the taste of longing is naturally self-evident, so why not think of a plan to seek a long-term cohabitation, how happy and sweet! But even this little bit cannot be done. From this point of view, they have no skill at all, and it is too clumsy for people to ask them for skill.

Words of a Famine Refugee 119

— Shijiu

The gate was accidentally left open, and suddenly a woman resembling a maidservant entered. She looked to be only in her forties, with a sallow complexion. Her clothes were not tattered, but she was wearing a half-worn summer cloth shirt. She was also carrying a bundle in one hand.

Reaching the courtyard, she opened her mouth and said in a low voice: "Madam, please give me some food." My sister-in-law looked her up and down and replied: "You don't look like someone who is begging for food, why did you suddenly break into my home?"

"Fleeing the famine"! These three words softly entered my ears, and I couldn't help but put down my newspaper and listen quietly to the woman's conversation.

She said: "Last year there was a drought, barely survived: then this year there was another flood, the people in the countryside really have no life left! The whole family is scattered in all directions; the two children have also been sold to others long ago. Arriving in Hangzhou, I originally hoped to find a bowl of rice to eat, but who knew..."

Before she finished speaking, my sister-in-law interjected, saying: "Helping others without pay, there must be someone who will take you, it is better than begging from door to door."

"There are so many intermediaries, I have been waiting for two days. Even the rice I had was from yesterday noon! Madam, please give me some food, I don't need any coins."

My sister-in-law was a little reluctant, so she asked the servant to serve her a bowl of rice and some pickles. The woman also asked for an old newspaper, wrapped the rice and pickles, thanked her, and left.

I watched her leave, feeling deeply melancholy. I remembered Chen Zilong's poem "Small Cart":

"The small cart is mottled, the yellow dust is late! The husband pushes, the wife pulls. Where are they going out? The green elm soothes my hunger, I wish to share gruel in a happy land. The wind blows the yellow wormwood, I see walls and houses, there must be a host who will feed you. I knock on the door, no one is home, the house has no pot, wandering empty streets, tears fall like rain!"

Comparing that to this, I think this famine refugee is still lucky.
